Important News Two

Case of Eight Murders Cracked in Shenyang 50

The net of heaven has large meshes, but it lets nothing through.

The souls of the wronged possess the murderer to confess.

The case of the cruel murder of eight people at the residence of Li Jingzhou, former Daoyin (Circuit Intendant) of Heilongjiang, in Haoran Lane, a commercial area in Shenyang, shocked the entire city more than ten days ago. The police authorities racked their brains and exhausted all means of investigation, but to no avail. Later, based on the report of Shang, the father-in-law of the deceased Li Peiqin (eldest son of Li Jingzhou), it was said that two people named You Qisan and Pi Guochen had been living in the Li household before the incident, and after the incident, the two disappeared. They were highly suspected, so detectives were dispatched separately. You Qisan was captured first, but his confession was ambiguous and no definite evidence was obtained. Subsequently, Pi Guochen was captured in Changtu, and he was immediately escorted to the provincial capital for interrogation. He confessed to the murder without denial, saying that he committed the crime together with You Qisan and another person named Deng Haiquan, and the reason was purely for revenge. After being detained, at about 11 o'clock in the evening, Bai Zijing, the Chief of the Public Security Bureau, fearing that there might be injustice even though the murderer had been arrested, personally interrogated Pi Guochen. Pi seemed to be half-asleep and his mind was wandering. Then he burst into tears, jumping and roaring wildly. The court police stopped him but he would not listen (the prisoner Pi was wearing heavy shackles on his feet, making it difficult to move, but he had such strength now, which was considered strange). He insisted on saying, "Let me kowtow to the Chief of the Department to seek justice and avenge my family! My whole family died so tragically!" Seeing this, Chief Bai ordered cold water to be splashed on his face to sober him up. After a while, prisoner Pi repeated his request, crying out more loudly, "Who are you?" he was asked. He replied, "I am Li Peiqin. I died so tragically! Please avenge me!" He also said, "All eight of us are here, kowtowing and begging!" After hearing this, Chief Bai and others were terrified and immediately ordered him to be taken back to prison and strictly ordered the arrest of Deng Haiquan for interrogation. At this time, prisoner Pi still seemed to be half-awake and his face was extremely ferocious. It is said that science is flourishing today and the talk of ghosts and gods is illusory and unfounded. But now, seeing this event, it proves that the saying "the wronged have a head and debts have an owner" is not false. The above was told to the reporter by a friend in the Public Security Bureau who witnessed the incident, and it was told with certainty, so it is specially recorded. It is also heard that when prisoner Pi was sober, he confessed that at about 11 o'clock that night, he and You and Deng committed the murder, one person handling the people in one room. Pi was the one who murdered Li Peiqin and his wife. After the incident, prisoner Pi returned to Changtu to live, but he always slept uneasily at night and his traces were occasionally revealed. If ghosts and gods are truly real, then the capture of Deng Haiquan is just around the corner.

Overseas Chinese in Russia Still Suffer Abuse 51

Recent Talks by Those Returning from Russia

Russia's New Communist System Implemented This Year

Russian Government Restricts Overseas Chinese from Returning Home

A Harbin dispatch on the 20th: Since the beginning of March, there have been four groups of overseas Chinese returning from Russia. The first group was 150 people, the second group was 86 people, the third group was 107 people, and the fourth group, which arrived in Harbin today, was 99 people. Regarding the abuse of overseas Chinese by the Russian side, from the Khabarovsk Agreement to the current Sino-Russian conference, our overseas Chinese are still living an inhuman life in foreign lands. According to the overseas Chinese who returned home today, they were all engaged in small businesses in the areas of Zeya and Chita in Russia. Before the Sino-Russian problem occurred, they had suffered all kinds of abuse from the Russian side. For example, when opening a store and obtaining a permit, they would be subjected to various difficulties by the officials. Unless a large amount of money was spent, the permit would never be obtained. After the business was established, there were various exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous levies, totaling at least three-fifths of the business income each month. Therefore, overseas Chinese, although nominally doing business, were actually like managers hired by others, suffering from the monthly oppression of shareholders. However, at that time, when returning home, they could still bring out (Chernetz)

200 Russian rubles. Since the incident on the Middle East Road, merchants have been arrested and imprisoned, and their property and goods have been confiscated. Since August 31, overseas Chinese in various places have been arrested and imprisoned one after another. The abuse in prison was even worse. As for food, 16 people were given one heavy loaf of black bread weighing three and a half jin per day, causing the strong, the young, and the old to suffer from hunger and emaciation. After being imprisoned for four months, they were released after the Khabarovsk agreement was reached. At that time, they had no home to return to and no place to live. Those who requested the Russian authorities to return the confiscated property were arrested and imprisoned again. Therefore, the overseas Chinese were afraid of the cruel prison life and would rather starve to death on the road than make any demands on the Russians. Recently, Russia has implemented a new communist system for a period of five years, confiscating privately owned property and returning it to the government. The government then provides food on a per capita basis, but those who do not work are still not allowed to eat. Workers are allowed to receive nine taels of black bread a day with a certificate and a monthly salary of more than ten yuan. This is only enough for a single person to support themselves. Families with several members often experience tragic events such as hanging and suicide. Public grievances are increasing day by day. Under such circumstances, overseas Chinese are discriminated against by the Russians regardless of whether they join the labor union or not. This is because after the war last year, the Russians felt that the Chinese communist elements were unreliable. At the same time, they are not as active as they were in the past in enticing Chinese to join the party. Since overseas Chinese in Russia are not allowed to do business or work, they have been thinking about returning home. However, fearing that the Chinese would expose the truth after returning home, the Russian side strictly restricts passports. Those who receive a passport to return home must pay taxes, ranging from hundreds of yuan, with no fixed amount and determined by the person. Therefore, some people have been applying for several months without success. There are more than 30,000 overseas Chinese in the areas of Chita and Verkhneudinsk. Because of the difficulty in obtaining passports and the lack of travel expenses, they cannot return home. Those who receive passports to return home are subjected to extremely strict inspections by the Red Russian military and police checkpoints along the way. At the 18-li Xiaozhan station on the border of Manchuria, they are subjected to strip searches, and their clothes and shoes are searched. If they carry even one Russian ruble, they will be sent back for detention. Therefore, overseas Chinese returning from Russia are penniless. When they arrive at Manzhouli in Chinese territory, fortunately, local organizations provide relief, giving each person one yuan for pocket money, one jin of white flour, and one sheng of millet.

Chairman of the Jiaojiao Railway Committee

Sa Fujun Arrives at the Bureau to Take Office 52

Qingdao dispatch: Sa Fujun, the newly appointed chairman of the Jiaoji Railway Committee, arrived in Qingdao at 2:00 p.m. on the 21st aboard the Shenwan ship. Senior officials in the bureau welcomed him at the pier. After exchanging greetings with the welcoming personnel, Mr. Sa went to the Qianhaiya Hotel to rest. Then, committee members Zhou Zhongqi, Cui Shijie, and Lu Mengxiong, accompanied him to the bureau and met with all the staff in the auditorium. Lu Mengxiong first gave a welcome speech on behalf of the committee. After the speech, Sa gave a speech, saying that since he was transferred to the ministry last year and separated from his colleagues, it has been nine months. While in the ministry, he often heard that the reorganization of the railway was progressing well, such as the repayment of Japanese debts, which had been determined with a plan, and the operating income had also increased compared to the past. The reconstruction of bridges and construction projects were being completed one after another. All of this was due to the efforts and diligence of his colleagues, which was greatly appreciated by the ministry. This time, Chairman Yan resigned from his post and went to Beijing. The ministry repeatedly tried to retain him, but Yan's intention to resign was firm and he was granted his request and continued to serve as a technical supervisor. He was ordered to come here. He considered himself to be incapable, but the committee members were mostly old friends. In the future, all matters should still be handled by the committee responsibly, and work together to plan for progress. He said that there are about two matters that should be paid attention to in the future regarding railway administration: 1. Employment. All colleagues serving here are serving the Jiaoji Railway, not serving private individuals. Even if the leader changes, the colleagues in office will not be transferred. The ministry adopts a talent-based approach to employing people on all roads, and specialized talents must be strongly protected. The law on the protection of technical personnel has already been promulgated. In addition, laws on the protection of vehicle affairs, accounting, and other personnel are also being drafted. It is hoped that all employees will work with peace of mind and not fail the ministry's good intentions to maintain them. 2. Finance. Although the operating income of the road has increased, the sharp increase in gold prices and the repayment of foreign debts have resulted in a budget deficit of more than 2 million yuan for the 19th year. In the future, financial resources must be conserved. However, saving is not just about reducing government administration and laying off employees. It is necessary to invest funds in profitable areas and not spend too much in the profit-sharing area. He hoped that his colleagues would pay close attention to this. It is heard that Mr. Sa will first come to the bureau to inspect matters starting today because the bureau is busy. The date of the formal swearing-in ceremony has not yet been determined (May 22).

Mining Law (Second Continuation) 53

Passed by the Legislative Yuan at the 88th Meeting

(Article 52) Before a state-owned mining right has been approved for lease by a private applicant, the local government with jurisdiction shall have the priority to lease it under equal conditions. If the applicants are both private individuals, the one who submitted the application to the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining first shall have the priority to lease it. (Article 53) The lessee may not sublease, mortgage, pawn, or transfer the state-owned mining right leased to him. (Article 54) The lease term for state-owned mining rights shall be limited to twenty years. If the state does not recover and operate the mine itself upon expiration, the lessee shall have the priority to continue leasing. The lessee shall pay rent annually in accordance with the following provisions: (1) If the net profit is less than 10% of the paid-up capital, no rent shall be paid. (2) If the net profit exceeds 10% of the paid-up capital but is within 35%, 50% of the excess shall be paid as rent. (3) If the net profit exceeds 35% of the paid-up capital, in addition to paying rent in accordance with the provisions of the preceding paragraph for the portion not exceeding 35%, 75% of the portion exceeding 35% shall be paid as rent. (Article 55) When the state recovers the mine for its own operation upon expiration of the lease term, it shall fairly evaluate and purchase the lessee's property or equipment applicable to the mining industry. If the state does not need to recover the mine upon expiration of the lease term, the original lessee shall be allowed to continue to enter into a contract for lease. (Article 56) In any of the following circumstances, the lease of the lessee shall be revoked immediately: (1) Violating the provisions of Article 52; (2) Failing to pay rent overdue; (3) Failing to engage in mine equipment within three years after leasing without justifiable reason; (4) Failing to start work or suspending work for more than one year after leasing without justifiable reason. (Article 57) When a lease is revoked due to any of the circumstances in the preceding article, the original lessee shall remove all ancillary property and equipment attached to the mining industry within six months, except for those belonging to the security scope or purchased by the state. However, this shall not apply if special circumstances have been submitted to the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining for approval. (Article 58) The provisions of Articles 14, 15, 16, 41, and 43 shall not apply to state-owned mining.

Chapter IV Small Mining (Article 59) Small mining rights may be established when one of the following circumstances is met: (1) Areas with inconvenient transportation that have been reported by the provincial competent authority and approved by the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining as small mining areas; (2) Mineral prospects are very small and have no value for large-scale operation; (3) Areas where the mining industry is underdeveloped and their mineral products are needed by the local area. The small mining area in the first item of the preceding paragraph may be canceled by the provincial competent authority upon request or when the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining deems it necessary. (Article 60) Small mining rights shall be limited to mining. (Article 61) No foreign capital may be added to small mining. (Article 62) Small mining rights shall be limited to ten years. After the expiration, the term may be extended for five years with approval if it does not hinder mining interests. However, if the circumstances stipulated in the first or third items of paragraph 1 of Article 59 are extinguished, the term may not be extended. The existence of small mining shall not hinder the application for mining rights. However, if the applied mining area overlaps with the small mining area, the small mining right holder shall be allowed to continue mining within the approved period, but the term may not be extended again after the expiration. (Article 63) Those who apply for the establishment of small mining rights shall submit an application with a mining area map to the provincial competent authority for approval, registration, and issuance of a small mining license, but shall also report to the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining for record. The small mining license in the preceding paragraph shall be issued by the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining in advance to the provincial competent authority. (Article 64) The Ministry of Agriculture and Mining may revoke the approval in the preceding article if it deems that it violates the provisions of Article 59. (Article 65) A small mining right holder shall have the priority to obtain mining rights when applying for the merger of small mining areas in accordance with the provisions of Article 36 within the time limit or within six months after the expiration of the time limit. (Article 66) The provisions of Articles 9, 15, 16, 95, 98, 99, and 101 shall not apply to small mining.

Chapter V Land Use (Article 67) The actual use of land for mining shall be for land use. (Article 68) Prospectors, mining applicants, or mining right holders may conduct surveys or inspections on other people's land when necessary, but must obtain permission from the local government where the land is located. When implementing surveys or inspections after obtaining the permission in the preceding paragraph, the land occupant shall be notified in advance. (Article 69) If it is necessary to remove obstacles due to surveys, inspections, etc., the consent of the land owner or land occupant shall be obtained. If the consent in the preceding paragraph cannot be obtained, the local government where the land is located shall be requested to permit the removal of the obstacles and notify the land owner or land occupant. (Article 70) Mining right holders may enter or use other people's land to defend against urgent mining risks, but shall immediately report to the local government where the land is located and notify the land owner or land occupant. (Article 71) If the land owner or land occupant suffers losses due to the circumstances in the preceding article, the prospector, mining applicant, or mining right holder shall provide appropriate compensation. (Article 72) If a mining right holder needs to use other people's land for mining purposes within 24 hours and does not harm the surface and its attachments, the land owner or land occupant shall be notified of the purpose of the use one day in advance. There shall be no refusal without justifiable reason. (Article 73) Mining right holders may use other people's land when necessary for one of the following reasons: 1. To excavate shafts and tunnels; 2. To stockpile mineral products, soil, rocks, explosives, firewood, charcoal, slag, ash, or all mining materials; 3. To build mining plants, warehouses, or other necessary buildings; 4. To establish large and small railways, transportation roads, canals, water pipes, steam pipes, ditches, ground wells, cableways, or power lines; 5. To install other various projects or works necessary for mining. (Article 74) The use of other people's land in accordance with the provisions of the preceding article shall be subject to the permission of the provincial competent authority and shall submit a construction plan with drawings and explanations for review and approval by the provincial competent authority. After the provincial competent authority grants the permission in the preceding paragraph, it shall immediately announce and notify the land owner and stakeholders. After the announcement or notification in the preceding paragraph, the mining right holder shall negotiate with the land owner and stakeholders to obtain the rights to the land. If the land is state-owned, the provincial competent authority shall seek the consent of the land manager before granting permission. The land area listed in Article 32 and the land area required for important public undertakings that the provincial competent authority has verified and recognized as not suitable for mining land shall not be permitted. (Article 75) Mining right holders shall not prohibit the necessary use of adjacent mining right holders within their mining area, except for those that must be used for mining without justifiable reason. (Article 76) When mining rights are transferred, the rights and obligations of land use shall be transferred at the same time. If mining rights are lost, the rights to use the land shall also be lost at the same time. (To be continued)

Wuhu Express News 54

Xiaodanyang Town in Dangtu is adjacent to Jiangning County. A few days ago, dozens of bandits suddenly came to the town. They started robbing at 9:00 a.m. and took the loot away at 3:00 p.m. Almost no businessman or resident in the town was spared from the huge losses. By the time the county government sent troops to suppress the bandits, they had gone far away. Two companies of the Wuhu Garrison Regiment were transferred from Digang yesterday to pursue the bandits.

There were many bandits hiding in Yuncao Town in Hanshan. They claimed to be the "Number One Army in the World." The Wuhu Garrison Regiment cracked their secret organization in the Dongji Hotel in Wubu, Wuhu. In addition to sending the arrested Chen Yufu and others to the capital for legal proceedings, they also sent troops to Yuncao to search for the bandits, but they had all fled upon hearing the news. Last night, the Military and Police Inspection Office and the Public Security Bureau successively arrested more than ten people, including Ding Changqing, in Henan and Liuchunyuan and other places. They were immediately sent to the regimental headquarters for interrogation.

Recently, bandits have also been found entrenched in the local area of Chaoxian, harassing the residents. According to reports, Battalion Commander Luo Yousheng of the Second Battalion of the Wuhu Garrison Regiment, led by Regiment Commander Lu, took soldiers on a small steamer yesterday to suppress the bandits.

Zhang Siwei, the magistrate of Wuwei County, previously initiated a joint defense of Wuhu with Wuwei, Fanchang, Luhe, Chaoxian, Hexian, and Hanshan Counties because bandits in southern Anhui were moving from one place to another to evade suppression. Now, Xuanzhou, Nanling, and Dangtu Counties, which are mostly adjacent to the counties, have also joined the joint defense, forming a ten-county joint defense. A joint bandit suppression meeting is planned to be held in Wuhu soon to eliminate the bandits. (24th)

Local Dispatch

Songjiang 55

Record of Hearing of a Family Lawsuit: The divorce case between Yang Shijie and Yang Chen Yunyu outside the East Gate has been appealed by Shijie to the Jiangsu High Court after the initial judgment was rejected. The court ordered a reconciliation, and both parties agreed and signed. They also stayed in the same room in a Suzhou hotel that night to reunite their dream of marriage. However, Yunyu's divorce decree was made clear. However, Yunyu was not satisfied with her husband's sister, Yang Cuilan, leaving home alone to stay at the Chengnian Women's School in the home of the clan chief, Yang Shen. The clothes, porcelain, bamboo, and wooden utensils that she had given were all in her husband's house. According to Gu A'mei, who was hired by Yang Cuilan, all the items were annihilated and destroyed by the eldest lady in order to accuse Yunyu of escaping with her luggage and instigate her younger brother Shijie to file for divorce. Yunyu, having learned of Cuilan's plot, went to the Women's Association to seek assistance. The association sent someone with the witness, Gu Xiaomei, to Yang's house for inspection. Cuilan was visiting Ning, and only her husband's younger brother, Bangjie, was left at home. According to the witness, Gu Xiaomei, the porcelain and copper utensils were pulled out of the well, which were Yunyu's belongings. Clothes and miscellaneous items were found in the house. Bangjie was supervised to take notes and everyone on the scene signed and handed them over to Bangjie for management. Yunyu, having obtained proof of Cuilan's concealment and slander, filed a criminal lawsuit with the county government, accusing Yang Cuilan of annihilating and damaging stolen goods. The case was previously summoned to collect original interrogations, ordered Yang Cuilan to post bail, and supplement witnesses. Yesterday (24th) was the first hearing, and the whole city was shocked. Five to six hundred people from far and near came to listen to the hearing. At 9:30 p.m., the court could not open the trial, so it was temporarily changed to a flower hall to set up seats for questioning. Du Cheng, the trial officer, summoned Yang Shen, the female clan chief, who said that Yunyu was her nephew's wife and had been oppressed by her husband's sister, Cuilan, even to the point of not giving her food. She had no choice but to stay temporarily in her house. She also stated that after the divorce reconciliation in the Suzhou High Court, the couple slept in the same bed in the hotel that night, which shows that there was no rift in the husband and wife's relationship. Unexpectedly, Shijie had another objection after returning home. Gu Xiaomei, the witness, testified that she worked in the eldest lady's (Cuilan) place, so she personally witnessed the concealment and damage of the plaintiff's dowry and clothing, but her conscience was disturbed, so she dared to testify about the damage to bamboo and wooden utensils and the location of concealment. After questioning, the defendant, Yang Cuilan, testified that she was 33 years old and still unmarried. She did not admit to any of the points accused by the plaintiff and pointed out that Yunyu did not have many dowry items, all of which had been taken away. When Yang Shijie was questioned, he also insisted that his wife had strange and inferior character and that all the points accused were false and fabricated. The sister and brother began to bow their heads and say nothing after being refuted one by one by the witnesses. The plaintiff firmly requested that the defendant be handed over to the questioning palace, advising Shijie that if the family was so discordant, he should not listen to one side of the story and oppress his wife. He also advised Yang Cuilan that because of her bad intentions and methods, she should be taken into custody, but she was leniently given five days to hand over the original items, otherwise she would be judged according to law. After the announcement, she was handed over to the original guarantor to leave the court, which was already late at twelve o'clock. However, Yang Cuilan's original guarantor was unwilling to take responsibility and changed to the local guarantor to watch over her before regaining her freedom this morning. The enthusiasm of the Song people for this case is unprecedented in recent years.

Seizure of Smuggling and Cross-Border Salt Inspection Ordered to Surrender Weapons: Wang Lisheng, the patrolling captain of the Kunshan anti-smuggling boat, led armed police to Shuangsui Township (12 li outside the West Gate) in Taicang yesterday afternoon (22nd, 5:00 p.m.) on the pretext of arresting smuggled salt and searched house to house, but found nothing. They also took illegal actions, causing public outrage. Both sides fought each other, resulting in Wang Lisheng being beaten and injured, and two out-of-town residents were also slightly injured. Later, the village chief and others of the township ordered them to surrender their weapons. At about 9:00 p.m., Wang and five other soldiers, four rifles, one Mauser pistol, and the injured out-of-town residents were all handed over to the county Public Security Bureau here. After questioning today, the bureau will transfer them to the judiciary for handling this afternoon.

Court Interrogation of the Case of a Crazy Uncle Killing His Sister-in-Law: Hua Bingci of this county was reported by County Magistrate Yuan through judicial procedures after he went mad and killed his sister-in-law with a knife. Yesterday, his mother sent Bingci to the case for questioning. The trial officer, Yang, questioned Hua, who talked about his experience of being stimulated in the same way as ordinary people, and his theory and opinions seemed to be even better than ordinary people. Afterwards, he began to talk incoherently. Later, the interrogating officer still ordered his mother to take him back for supervision.

Wang Jinsun Beaten to Death: Wang Jinsun, a farmer in Beitashiqiao, Qingpu, had been married to his wife, Ni, for several years. The couple had always been harmonious. Recently, Wang suffered from madness and acted like an idiot, beating his wife all day long, leaving her covered in injuries. On the previous day, Wang used a hemp rope to tie his wife's throat, causing her to be strangled to death. The township chief reported the case to Pan, the director of the Huangdu Public Security Bureau. After receiving the report, he immediately sent police to arrest Wang and reported it to the county government for inspection. The inspection confirmed that she had been beaten and strangled to death before her death. Wuxi 60

Gunshots and Shadows of Blood Before Miao Bin's Residence: Inside the South Gate of this County, under the Bianmin Bridge, the front and rear gates of the mansion of Miao Bin, former Director of the Civil Affairs Department of Jiangsu Province, are guarded. The police officers on duty last night from 9:00 PM to 12:00 AM were Song Shaolun, a first-class policeman from the First Public Security Bureau (at the front gate of the Miao residence), and Meng Jie, a police trainee (at the rear gate of the Miao residence). About half an hour after they took over, two thugs dressed in short clothes came to the front gate of the Miao mansion and talked with the guard Song Shaolun for a while. Suddenly, the two thugs took out pistols and opened fire on Song Shaolun, hitting him in the right chest, penetrating the lung, and exiting from the back. After being injured, Song pulled out his Mauser pistol to fight back, but the two thugs fired another shot, hitting the left (south) side of the glass window of the nearby Puren Hospital's clinic. Song also returned fire, firing two shots in succession, but both missed. Song then rushed to the Liedi Temple to report to the police station. Because of excessive bleeding and severe pain from his injuries, he collapsed. Guo Xikun, a policeman on duty under the Nanshi Bridge, sent him to Puren Hospital for treatment and rushed to the police station to report. Patrol Chief Xu Yunsheng led police officers to pursue the attackers. At the same time, Magistrate Sun received the report and immediately ordered the closure of all city gates and implemented martial law. He personally led the police force to search for the thugs. Huang Zhenquan, Director of the Public Security Bureau, Mao Mujun, Director of the Water Police District, and others also led detectives to investigate everywhere, but the two thugs had already fled far away, and nothing was gained. Police officer Song Shaolun's injuries are quite serious. According to general speculation, the thugs did not seem to be robbers intending to steal property, but rather came specifically to seek revenge on Song Shaolun.

Tragic News of a Cargo Ship Robbed in Taihu Lake: Xu Jianshan (63 years old), a resident of Xu Lane, Ninety-ninth Tu, Fourteenth District (Kaihua Township) of this county, has been operating a general merchandise and meat store called Xu Xichang in Suzhou Dongting Xishan Luzhu, transporting goods back and forth on the lake for more than ten years. On the 15th of this month, Xu Jianshan took the Xihu steamer back to Wuxi to purchase goods. On the 19th, he hired Shao Qiaosheng (53 years old), a lake boatman, from Wanbu Port in this township to sail to Xishan Luzhu. Shao, along with his eldest son Guoqing (23 years old), second son Qiqing (7 years old), and Xu Jianshan, a total of four people, loaded 14.5 shi of white rice, 2 dan of soybeans, 2 dan of soybean oil, 2 dan of soy sauce, 4 jars of shochu, and 8 large pigs onto the boat. At 10:00 AM, they set sail from Zigang and exited the port. Unexpectedly, while traveling on the lake near Raozhu, they were suddenly robbed by lake bandits, suffering heavy losses. Xu Jianshan and the boatmen Shao Qiaosheng, Guoqing, and Qiqing were all killed. The Xu family was alarmed upon hearing the news. Until the day before yesterday, the Xu family received a special report from the Wuxikou Lifesaving Bureau stating that an ownerless sunken boat was found there. Bloodstains were found all over the boat, and there were also four pairs of shoes of various sizes. Yesterday, Xu Jianshan's son, Quanfu, filed a complaint with the Public Security Bureau, requesting the pursuit and arrest of the murderers, and also placed an advertisement to search for the bodies.

Verdict in the Case of Forcible Rape of a Virgin: Xi Aqin (16 years old), daughter of Xi Ronglin, a villager from the Qiantoutou Township of Yanqiao Town in this county, worked at the Minfeng Silk Factory outside the South Gate. On April 1st, she was tricked by Fan Qinsheng (nickname "Big Hand Aqi"), a fellow villager, to the Luhai Inn on the road, where he raped her. After her father, Xi Ronglin, learned of this, he twisted Fan and took him to the Fifth District Office, who transferred him to the county government for detention. Yesterday afternoon, Examining Officer Zhou Cheng summoned Xi Aqin and her father, Xi Ronglin, to court for interrogation. Xi Aqin testified, "I was indeed raped by him." Fan Qinsheng testified, "It was not rape, Aqin willingly had an affair with me," etc. Mr. Zhou reviewed the testimonies and reasoned that raping a 16-year-old girl, even consensual intercourse, is considered rape. Therefore, he sentenced Fan Qinsheng to seven years of imprisonment.

Changzhou 61

Silkworm Cocoon Markets in Various Townships Open One After Another: The silkworm cocoon markets in various townships of Wuyi opened one after another on the 23rd and 24th. An investigation of cocoon prices in various places showed that they ranged from 45 to 50 yuan. According to the usual practice in previous years, the price of cocoons of inferior quality was also collected at the beginning of the market, and the price of small, better quality cocoons also increased gradually. This year, the color of the silk is not good, so the goods will not be piled up. It is expected that the price will rise in the future. The most lively cocoon market in this county is the Northeast Township. The three companies of Qishuyan Taijiang Fuchang and Li Tongyi in that area opened on the 24th, and the cocoon price was collected up to 50 yuan, but the goods were not yet crowded. The cocoon prices and collection situation of the cocoon markets near Hengshan Bridge are the same as those in Qishuyan. The Zhengda Cocoon Market in Hetou Bridge borrowed 50,000 yuan from the Wuxi Zhenyi Silk Factory to rent and collect cocoons. It opened on the 24th and collected more than 50 dan of fresh cocoons, at a general price of 51 yuan per dan.

Further Appointment of the Post Office Director: Zhang Yunwen, the second-class post office director of Wuyi County, recently received an order from the Jiangsu Postal Administration to transfer him and further appoint Cheng Taoshi as his replacement. Cheng took office on the 21st. The Administration sent a letter to the County Government yesterday (the 24th) to inform them.

Nantong 64

Organization of a Provisional Defense Committee: The bandit situation in the four townships of Nantong is becoming increasingly severe. On the 24th, representatives from various local circles held an emergency meeting at the General Chamber of Commerce in the county seat, chaired by County Magistrate Zhang. It was decided to organize a provisional defense committee to plan the defense of the entire county and eliminate bandits, communists, and all reactionary elements. Thirty-six people, including Li Yinong, were designated as committee members, divided into five sections: general affairs, planning, finance, intelligence, and publicity. Defense committees will be established in each district within a specified time. The committee's expenses and all bandit suppression costs will be jointly borne, managed, and disbursed by businesses and wealthy individuals in each district. The committee will be dissolved after local order is restored.

Civil Affairs Department Team to Suppress Bandits: The Civil Affairs Department, because areas such as San Yi and Si Yu in Nantong are troubled by self-proclaimed Red Army bandits, has transferred provincial police teams to concentrate in Nantong and eliminate them within half a month.

Jinsha's Special Martial Law to Defend Against Bandits: Jinsha has been unsettled by bandits in recent days. The military and police have implemented special martial law and captured a bandit scout, Yu Jinsheng, in Qiantou Town, who was immediately executed by firing squad.

Jiaxing 66

Continuing Interrogation of the Gang-Related Kidnapping Organization Smashed in Puyuan: The Hangzhou Provincial Public Security Bureau's detective team uncovered a kidnapping organization in a thatched shed near Yangjia Bang in the western part of Puyuan Town, Jiaxing, and rescued one hostage. Two bandits were arrested on the spot, and wooden-cased guns and pistols were seized. Later, two female bandits were arrested at the home of a Guixing in the West Market of Puyuan Town. All the witnesses who were arrested were taken to Hangzhou to be interrogated. According to an investigation, the hostage was indeed a person from Dayun, Jiashan, who was kidnapped at the end of last year. A letter was sent to his family, and after several negotiations, a ransom of 10,000 yuan was required. It is said that 7,000 yuan had already been paid somewhere, and the remaining 3,000 yuan was scheduled to be paid at a hotel in Hangzhou this month. Initially, the hostage was hidden in another place, but at the beginning of March, he was moved to a hole in the thatched shed. Wax candle oil was poured into both ears to prevent him from hearing sounds. The detective team obtained a clue from a certain source and arrested the bandits in Puyuan. The kidnappers fired guns in the thatched shed to resist arrest. The detectives also fired back. Eventually, the kidnappers were defeated and arrested. The hostage was found in the hole. The hostage had suffered greatly in the hole, so he was like a wooden chicken and his nerves had become abnormal. The thatched shed at that location has already been burned down.

Shangyu 67

The Establishment of the Zhangzhen Embankment Affairs Bureau is Unlikely: The embankments in Zhangzhen, including Basha, Qishan, and Jiulian Wantou, protect thousands of acres of farmland. Their situations are actually interconnected. However, the division of responsibilities and the lack of mutual assistance spirit among the directors, the temporary donations, the absence of savings in the hands of the embankment owner, and the lack of disaster prevention preparations mean that the entire town is located in a low-lying area. Once flooded, it becomes a major disaster. County Magistrate Zhang Jingxu had previously inspected the town and believed that it was of great importance to the people's livelihood. He advocated setting up an embankment affairs bureau to take on its responsibility, so that it could gather the strength of the masses to easily accomplish the task. He presented a request to the provincial authorities and approved 3,000 yuan to subsidize the embankment expenses. He also extended an invitation to many embankment directors in the town to attend a meeting to discuss future strategies. However, no embankment director attended the second scheduled meeting. Zhang was quite indignant that the establishment of the embankment affairs bureau was unlikely.

The Chinese Basketball Team Was Again Defeated by the Philippines

The Philippines Won Because of Accurate Long Throws

(1) Each Scored 19 Points in the First Half

Tokyo, 25th (Our Report) The Chinese basketball team was defeated by Japan for the first time. Last night at 8:00 PM, it was poisoned by the Philippines again. The championship of this game has been declared hopeless. In last night's China-Philippines game, the Philippines won 39 to 34. In the first half, the score was tied at 19. In the second half, the Philippines scored five more points to win the final victory. Thousands of spectators were extremely excited. China and the Philippines each had cheerleading squads to cheer each other and boost morale. The Philippines' victory depended on the accuracy of its long throws. China's Lu Zhong'en missed opportunities under the enemy's basket time and time again. The whole game was clean and agile. As soon as the whistle sounded, both sides hunted each other. Two minutes later, the Philippines' McLina scored the first point. Liu Jianchang returned a point. Yao Enhan made a free throw. Since then, the Philippines' momentum suddenly increased. McLina was the giant of their team. Tang Yao found it difficult to monitor his activities. Liu Jianchang tried to throw from a distance many times, and all of them were successful, resulting in twelve equal scores. Cheers from the audience shook the whole venue, rising and falling. Each side scored 19 points in the first half.

Bird's-Eye View of the Venue 110

The 9th Far Eastern Games were held in Tokyo, Japan. The Japanese side not only made special efforts in various competitions, selecting strong teams in order to defeat China and the Philippines and dominate the Far East, but also strived for excellence in all aspects of layout, equipment, hospitality, and publicity. The construction of the venue was particularly costly, magnificent, and truly spectacular. It cannot be compared to the sports fields on Shanghai's Avenue Dubail and Hangzhou's Mei Dong Gaoqiao.

Track and Field Venue 111

The Far Eastern Games venue is located in Meiji Jingu Gaien, about ten miles from the center of Tokyo. It can be reached by car from Tokyo Station in about 20 minutes. The air near the venue is excellent, with wide roads and trees planted on both sides, lush green grass like a lawn, quiet and pleasant, quite similar to the area of Shanghai French Concession's Avenue Baille. The width of the road is almost double. Cars drive without dust and there is no worry of congestion. In addition, Japanese women in elegant clothes walk in groups, adding to the scenery and making it more interesting. At the end of the wide road is the Painting Hall, a magnificent building. Shortly after heading west, you can see the track and field venue in the shade of the trees. The scale of the venue is entirely based on the construction of the International Sports Stadium. The rostrum and spectator stands on one side are all made of cement. The national flags of the four countries are hung high on the rostrum and in the center of the venue. The press seats are on both sides of the board of directors' seats. The other half of the circle opposite the rostrum is a natural grandstand made of earth. It is extremely clear to see the actions of people in the field. The entire venue can accommodate about 50,000 people. The soccer field is located inside the track and field, and the track and field events do not conflict in time.

Basketball and Volleyball Venue 112

About a dozen steps south of the track and field venue is the basketball and volleyball venue. It was originally a Japanese open wrestling venue, which has been processed and transformed. The surrounding is a natural green grass grandstand. From a distance, it looks very much like a bowl-shaped stadium. The ball court is 80 feet long and 40 feet wide. The wooden boards are made of American pine. The basketball hoop legs have small wheels and can be moved freely. Open boxing matches are also held here. There are several vertical and horizontal wires and dozens of electric lights above it, illuminating the night like daytime. The entire venue can accommodate 15,000 people.

Filipino athletes arrive at Tokyo Station

Baseball Field 113

Adjacent to the basketball and volleyball venue is the baseball field. The Japanese are almost household names for baseball. The Japanese Six University Baseball Championship is held here. The venue is extremely wide and the grandstand can accommodate 70,000 to 80,000 people. It is conceivable how large the venue is.

New Swimming Pool 114

This time, the Japanese Swimming Competition Committee, in view of Japan's failure at the 8th Far Eastern Games, has made special efforts in the training of athletes. It is very confident in winning the championship. In order to promote swimming, it allocated US$250,000 to build a large swimming pool and a diving pool in the open space slightly north and behind the track and field venue. From April 20th, work was carried out day and night to rush construction. As of the time the reporter filed this report, it has not yet been completed. The construction of the large grandstand has only been completed by 60-70%. According to the people of the Japan Sports Association, the swimming competition should be completed before any event. In addition, the tennis court is not in one place, which is a pity. (Qian Hua, May 19)

Japanese Newspapers Boast About Basketball Victory 115

Not a Word About Unfair Judging

Chinese Team Has a Spirit of Benevolence and Chivalry

This newspaper, Tokyo, 25th: This morning, Japanese newspapers, without exception, used eye-catching headlines to greatly boast about the Japanese basketball team's first victory over China last night. All credited the victory to the team members' careful and courageous fighting and outstanding offense and defense. Not a single word was mentioned about the unfairness of the referees. In fact, only four of the twelve fouls charged against our country could be justified. Our team members were in such a disadvantageous position that they almost lost the possibility of activity. The Japanese team's ball skills have indeed improved compared to previous years, but the referees' slightest partiality immediately changed the overall situation. Moreover, in the situation like yesterday, even if our country's coaches and players were determined to save the situation, it may not have been possible. However, yesterday, although our country lost, all the team members were able to maintain the spirit of sportsmen. When the Japanese were overjoyed with their first victory over us and sang the national anthem loudly, our team members still forgot the previous disappointment and stood up in unison to show respect to Japan. This kind of spirit left a deep impression on the audience at the time.

Sidelines of the Games (Qian Hua) 116

Reporters rushed around. Japanese newspapers paid extraordinary attention to sports news and covered sports news in great detail. The Japanese Youth Hall became the target of everyone. Almost every moment, reporters from various newspapers could be seen doing their interviews separately, either interviewing the Philippine soccer team or talking to our baseball team. The first difficulty was the language barrier. Every word and every sentence required the assistance of a translator. The Japanese translator of the Youth Hall is now an ordinary shop assistant. His knowledge is extremely limited, and he often does not know what he is talking about at all. A reporter from a Kyushu newspaper went to the second floor to find our country's staff. Rong Qizhao received him. The reporter said that he wanted to talk to the baseball team representative about the situation of your country's baseball team. Rong said that if there were any questions, he could answer them on their behalf. Because the team came from the United States, they only spoke English and Cantonese. The translator only knew Shanghainese, which was quite difficult. (The reporter still insisted on seeing them, and after a long time, he could not get his way. Finally, he asked about the strength of the Chinese and Philippine baseball teams. Rong said that you can't know until you play. He also asked what the Chinese baseball team members thought of the Japanese baseball team's criticism of Miyata's skills. Rong replied that he had already learned about it in the university battle a few days ago. It was very good, very good. The interview ended.) Another day, a reporter from a newspaper asked about the brief history of our country's head representative, Zhang Boling. He was told that he was currently the president of Nankai University in Tianjin and was quite prestigious in the education field. The next morning, the newspaper prominently published that Zhang Boling had served as Minister of Education. There were all kinds of absurdities, all caused by the language barrier.

100-Meter Time 117

Ms. Sun Guiyun, the well-known track and field athlete, was also very popular in Japan. Various newspapers praised her extremely favorably, praising her as second only to Kinu. It can be seen that the Japanese admire heroes. Ms. Sun would return to her room on the second floor of the Youth Hall to rest after practicing in the field every morning. Someone brought a large, solitary Asahi Shimbun sports special issue, which contained detailed records of Japanese women's track and field achievements. This aroused the female earth's great attention and frequently asked about Kinu's 100 meters. She asked what her results were. She replied that among the ten best Japanese women runners, Kinu ranked first with a score of 12 seconds. The tenth place had a score of 13.4 seconds. Ms. Sun said after hearing this, "I know they run very fast." It contains quite a bit of sour grapes.

Iron Bed Load 118

Mr. Zhang Boling, the head representative of our country, is of a towering and unusually tall stature, worthy of the northern athletes. Initially, he had intended to live in the Japanese Youth Hall, but later he felt that it was too noisy, so he moved to the Marunouchi Hotel. At that time, the hotel was already full, and only a small room in a corner on the fifth floor was left. The Secretary Zhang of the Youth Association accompanied him to the room. The furnishings in the room consisted only of a medium-sized iron bed and a table and two chairs. Secretary Zhang saw that the iron bed was not large and that Dr. Zhang's weight was also unusually heavy, so he was worried that it would not be able to bear the load. He quickly said, "This bed is too small, right?" Dr. Zhang said, "Although my body is big, it's not to that extent."

Filipino athletes arrive at Tokyo Station

The first place in shot put, Japanese Takada Shizuo

Useless Place to Display Talents 119

After the Chinese athletes arrived in Tokyo, they did not exchange Japanese currency in a hurry, and no shop in Tokyo accepted Chinese currency. As a result, the athletes all cried out in suffering, opening their eyes to the money but having nowhere to use it. It was truly a situation of "heroes having no place to display their talents." They jointly requested the representative to find a solution. Finally, a certain gentleman from the Yokohama Consulate personally went to Yokohama to change it. In total, he exchanged more than 4,000 Japanese yen.

Breaking the Budget 120

The cost of living in Japan has soared in recent years, almost on par with Europe and the United States. Normally, it costs four Japanese angles to wash a suit shirt and one angle for socks. Each pair of cotton trousers costs one yuan. The Chinese athletes run around and practice every day, sweating like a slurry, and almost have to change their clothes every day. Basketball coach Dong Shouyi quickly calculated that it was not economically feasible. He hurriedly said to the basketball team members, "It's best if you can wash your small items yourselves, otherwise change them less often. If everyone goes to wash them at will, the laundry fee will cost 5,000 Japanese yen, which would break the budget." It can also be seen the cost of living in Japan.

Government Preserves National Games Results 124

After the conclusion of the National Games, Chairman Dai Jitao, considering that the construction costs of the venue and dormitory were huge, and that it would be inappropriate to preserve them as a waste of money, proposed three measures for disposal. The proposal was approved by the government and sent to the Executive Yuan, which ordered the Ministry of Education, the Ministry of Military Affairs, the Ministry of Finance, and the Zhejiang Provincial Government to comply. The three measures are as follows: (1) The Zhejiang Provincial Government will bear half of the costs. (2) A barracks and playground of equal size to the current playground will be constructed. The expenses will be borne equally by the National Government and the Zhejiang Provincial Government. (2) The current sports field will be designated as the National Hangzhou Sports Field and handed over to the Education Department of the Zhejiang Provincial Government for management. (3) Before the establishment of the aforementioned construction, the current sports field will be temporarily allocated for military use. The sports construction on the ground will be the responsibility of the Zhejiang Provincial Education Department.

Important News

Jiangsu Education Department Orders to Organize 125

Preliminary Education and Expenditure Distribution Standards in Various Counties

The Jiangsu Provincial Education Department instructed the directors of education bureaus in various counties, saying that in order to comply with the matter, the development of local education depends entirely on whether the educational funds and the facilities are balanced. To spend wastefully with funds and to be extravagant without funds, both are enough to lead to the bankruptcy of local education. Whenever the semester ends in each county, elementary school principals or city medical personnel often disregard whether the educational funds are sufficient, requesting to add levels and establish schools, or asking people to intercede, or gathering crowds to surround, or arbitrarily adding levels and establishing schools. In the middle of the semester, they forcibly request the Education Bureau to bear the expenses or arbitrarily increase the salaries of teachers and school expenses. There are even other public officials who force the establishment of schools in order to introduce private individuals. There are also those who falsely claim that the expenses can be raised by themselves in order to seek private gain under the guise of public interest. If the responsible bureau delays slightly, they will say that it is destroying education, and if they are not recognized, they will recklessly attack. Counting the matters of each county where the increase in education expenditure has led to bankruptcy, and the director has suffered hardship because he has performed his duties and abided by the law, the ultimate cause is that this kind of out-of-track action is the root of the problem. Now the eighteenth year is coming to an end, and the nineteenth year is about to begin. All the counties should follow the outline of the educational budget that has been ordered to follow and formulate the education budget for the nineteenth year. All counties where the existing educational undertakings exceed the annual budget income should follow the outline and earnestly reduce or merge them. From now on, the addition of levels and the establishment of schools in each county should be supervised by the county magistrate and the director of the education bureau according to the results of the administrative meters and the consideration of the balance of funds and undertakings. They should properly formulate plans and submit them to the Education Department for review and decision. As for the distribution of school funds, compulsory education should be the main body. Before the junior high schools and the higher grades of elementary schools have made other special funds, no expansion is allowed. The annual fee for each grade in the higher grades of elementary schools should be between 500 yuan and 700 yuan, and the number of teachers should be one and a half. The annual fee for each grade in the junior grades and the junior elementary schools should be between 200 yuan and 350 yuan, and the number of teachers should be one. Each county should formulate distribution standards in detail according to the above-mentioned limits, but still according to the original standards and economic capacity of the county, and submit them together with the budget book for examination. Those whose original standards are less than the above-mentioned minimum limits shall not be allowed to increase without authorization before special funds are approved. The tuition fees collected by all schools should be handed over to the bureau for official use and included in the budget income. The number of students should be 50. For those who exceed or fall short, the regular expenses should be increased or decreased. If the classrooms are small, a two-part teaching system should be implemented. If there are not enough 30 people, classes are not allowed to be opened. Of the fees added for each grade in the junior section due to the number of people exceeding the quota, 80% shall be the labor performance salary of the head teacher of each grade, and 20% shall be miscellaneous expenses. The principal shall not use the excuse of the contract to move it privately. If assistant teachers need to be hired in each grade, the recommendation of the head teacher of each grade must be obtained, and the permission of the principal or the person in charge and the education committee or the principal of the central elementary school must be obtained, and the principal shall appoint him. The salary shall be paid from the labor performance salary that the head teacher should receive, and no other public funds shall be paid. The decision on the number of people in each grade each semester shall be based on the average number of attendances during the inspection by administrative personnel more than once. However, if there are indeed children with grades in the school that can prove that there are actually people there, they can also be recognized. Before the number of grades in each school is decided at the beginning of the school year, the public expenses paid by each school each month shall be provisionally supported and then settled clearly after the decision is made. Official expenses must be used to the fullest extent possible, and people must be used to the fullest extent possible, so that the effect of the school can be maximized. At the same time, the individual's gains shall be slightly surplus, and the total amount of public expenditure shall not be drastically increased, so that administrative progress can be gradually expected. All the above-mentioned items shall be strictly enforced by the county magistrate together with the director of the education bureau, and there shall be no favoritism. The education expenditure budget for the nineteenth year of each county shall be prepared and submitted for review before the end of June of this year. In particular, the expenditure of universal education funds must be carried out in strict compliance with the law. If there is any violation of the above instructions, only the director of the education bureau of each county shall be questioned. In addition to the order, you should immediately follow and announce it to the public. This order is of utmost importance.

Current Conditions of Party Education in Various Schools in This City 128

The Training Department of the Shanghai Special City Party Headquarters considers the promotion of Party Doctrine education during the Tutelage Period to be of utmost importance. Therefore, it is customary to conduct a Party Education inspection once every semester to assess achievements and make improvements accordingly. The department's Party Doctrine Education Section has decided during its Third Section Affairs Meeting that the third inspection will commence from June 1st for middle schools and from June 5th for primary schools, concluding approximately one month later. This inspection of middle schools will be handled by the Party Doctrine Education Section of the department. All other more than five hundred public and private primary schools will be assigned to districts for inspection based on location. The fourth grade of primary schools must undergo testing to observe their actual level of understanding. It is reported that all inspection forms and documents have been distributed to the respective districts. The district training committees will organize Party Education inspection committees to prepare everything. All schools within the city should also prepare early. Schools that received supervision, urging, or warnings during the second inspection last year should pay particular attention in advance, it is said.

Local News

Foreign Minister Wang Temporarily Will Not Return to Beijing 130

Fan Guangzhi's Statement

The Guomin News Agency reports that Fan Guangzhi, a counselor of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, who brought a letter from President Tan and others urging Foreign Minister Wang to return to Beijing, was previously reported. Yesterday, a reporter from the Guomin News Agency interviewed Mr. Fan and inquired about when Foreign Minister Wang would return to Beijing to cancel his leave. He replied as follows: Minister Wang has felt quite fatigued after working hard to recover Vladivostok and sign the Sino-Japanese tariff agreement and other important cases, so he wanted to take some time to rest. He previously requested a two-week leave from President Tan for recuperation. However, President Tan and other central figures believed that foreign affairs were important and could not be without someone in charge for a day, so they all advised him to return to Beijing to handle matters as soon as possible. Chairman Chiang also telegraphed Minister Wang, urging him to return to Beijing. Minister Wang originally intended to return to Beijing with the spirit of dedicating himself to the country, but according to doctors, Minister Wang's intestinal illness is quite severe, and his stomach often feels acidic and vomits due to parasites in his intestines. He must receive ten days of treatment before he can recover. Therefore, Minister Wang has no choice but to continue his leave and cannot return to Beijing temporarily. The reporter further inquired about the recent progress of foreign affairs. According to the reply, since American Minister Johnson came to Shanghai, there has been progress in discussing the issue of abolishing consular jurisdiction. The embassies of Norway, Cuba, Finland, Czechoslovakia, and Turkey in Peiping have all moved south. The Japanese embassy has also moved its seals and important documents. The German embassy will also move after finding suitable housing in Beijing and Shanghai. The reactionary warlords in the north wanted to bewilder the foreign envoys in order to achieve their conspiracy to restrain the central government, but now they have nothing to rely on. The reporter asked Mr. Fan when he would return to Beijing. Fan said that he must return to Beijing tonight to report to President Tan, President Hu, and others.

A Total of Forty-Two People

Then, representatives from the Social Affairs Bureau arrived at the scene and distributed three dimes of food money per person according to their names. Organizational Rules for Social Groups 138

Announced by the Civic Training Association

The Full Text Contains Fourteen Articles

Article 1 of the Organizational Rules for Social Groups in Shanghai Special City, formulated by the Mass Training Committee of the Shanghai Special City Executive Committee, was passed by the 7th Committee Meeting of the association and announced yesterday for implementation. The original text is as follows:

Organizational Rules for Social Groups in Shanghai Special City (Article 1) Social groups referred to in these rules include student groups, women's groups, religious groups, charity groups, cultural groups, and hometown associations, etc. (Article 2) To initiate the organization of a social group, there must be five or more initiators residing in this city with legitimate businesses. They must jointly nominate representatives, prepare a written statement of reasons and resumes of the initiators (resumes can be obtained from this association), and submit the original and duplicate copies to this association for permission. (Article 3) After accepting the application, this association will send personnel to inspect its main points: (1) Whether the reasons presented are legitimate and factual; (2) Whether the purpose is pure; (3) Whether the members are loyal; (4) Whether there is a similar organization; (5) Whether there is a need for organization. (Article 4) If the inspection is deemed qualified, in addition to the approval, a permit will be issued and a letter will be sent to the Social Affairs Bureau or the Municipal Education Bureau for reference. (Article 5) After the initiators receive the approval from this association, they should immediately send personnel to the association to collect the permit. (Article 6) After the initiators obtain the permit, they shall appoint preparatory members to organize a preparatory committee, engrave the preparatory association's seal according to the name approved by this association. The style should be one inch and five points square on a carpenter's ruler, with two points on each side, and the text should read (Preparatory Committee of the Shanghai Special City [Name of the Association]), using regular script, and submit the activation date and seal to this association and the competent government for record. Student groups and cultural groups are subject to the supervision of the Education Bureau and the Social Affairs Bureau. (Article 7) The preparatory period for social groups is limited to one month for student groups, two months for religious, cultural, and women's groups, and six months for charity groups after the preparatory committee is filed for approval. (Article 8) After the preparation is completed, the proposed draft of the association's charter and the membership list should be submitted to this association for review (the association's charter and membership list should be copied on paper obtained from the association). (Article 9) The association's charter should specify the following items: (1) Name; (2) Purpose; (3) Area and address of the association; (4) Qualifications of members and their rights and obligations; (5) Regulations for members' admission, withdrawal, and expulsion; (6) Number of officials, their powers, and regulations for retirement and removal; (7) Regulations for meetings; (8) Regulations for membership fees and other accounting; (9) Regulations for mutual assistance; (10) Regulations for amendments to the charter; (16) Regulations for dissolution and liquidation. (Article 10) After the association's charter is approved by this association, a founding meeting should be convened and a request should be made to this association to send personnel for guidance. (Article 11) After the social group is established, a list of important officials of the association should be filled out (the form must be in accordance with the regulations of this association), and changes to the charter and membership list should be reported to this association. After the inspection is deemed sound, this association will issue an order to the association for certification and send a letter to the Social Affairs Bureau or the Education Bureau for reference. (Article 12) After receiving the above-mentioned approval, the social group should immediately apply for registration with the competent government. (Article 13) If a social group has any of the following circumstances, it should request this association for approval for record at any time: (1) The date of the members' meeting or representatives' meeting; (2) Re-election of officials; (3) Admission and withdrawal of members; (4) Collection of special funds, temporary fundraising, or shares; (5) Punishment or expulsion of members; (6) Reorganization or dissolution; (7) Amendments to the charter. (Article 14) These rules shall be announced and implemented by this association.

The Fifth Propaganda Meeting of the Municipal Propaganda Department 139

The Shanghai Special City Party Headquarters Propaganda Department held its fifth municipal propaganda meeting yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM. The attendees included Chen Dezheng, Bao Rong, Xu Xingchu from the Municipal Propaganda Department, and Shen Yu, Shen Risheng, Diao Qing'en, Yang Shaozhi, Huang Xianggu, and other district propaganda commissioners, totaling more than ten people. Request the Municipal Propaganda Department to instruct each district to uniformly comply. 2. The district party headquarters or district sub-headquarters near each distribution point should uniformly post propaganda signs. (3) The improvement plan for periodic publications in each district should be submitted by the deadline. The Municipal Party Headquarters to Establish a Trade Union Secretary Training Institute 140

The Mass Training Committee of the Shanghai Special City Party Headquarters, in view of the importance of trade union secretary training, plans to open a trade union secretary training institute next month. The plan and its budget have been approved by the Municipal Executive Committee and Comrade Pan Gongzhan has been appointed as the director of the training institute. The original text of the plan is copied below: (1) Origin: The labor movement in this city has always been developed. The number of trade unions registered with Party and government agencies has reached more than 300. However, their quality still cannot fully meet our ideals. The majority of trade union members still need the Party's expedited training. The Civic Training Association believes that although there are many ways to train, the trade union secretary who guides and delves into the grassroots level to share the responsibility of leading the masses will surely achieve great results. However, at present, there are still few trade union secretaries with excellent talents and hardworking work. Most of the secretaries, those above can only draft documents and manage records; those in the middle waste association funds sitting idly; those below either flatter the capitalists and contribute to the workers, or collude with bandits and instigate unrest. The harm is incalculable. The Civic Training Association is angry and worried about it, so the Trade Union Secretary Training Institute was established, and the Trade Union Secretary Training Committee is in charge of its affairs. Within a year and a half, several sound secretaries will be created and sent to various trade unions to take office. (2) Training Objectives: This institute focuses on political education, health education, livelihood education, leisure education, language and writing education, and social interaction education for trade union secretaries. The graduates should possess the following conditions in the future: (1) Understand and believe in the Three Principles of the People; (2) Understand ordinary social sciences; (3) Understand the international situation and the oppression imposed on us by the great powers; (4) Understand the various laws and regulations related to the labor movement and have a rudimentary knowledge of law; (5) Develop the ability to use the four powers; (6) Be able to serve as a coach for the Boy Scouts; (7) Have knowledge and skills in common first aid; (8) Be able to organize various cooperatives; (9) Be able to play games such as football, basketball, and tennis; (10) Be able to speak in public and preside over meetings; (11) Be able to write articles and draw pictures; (12) Have the spirit of serving the community; (13) Have the willingness and habit of approaching workers; (14) Have the ability to educate workers. (3) Organization: The organization of this institute is as follows: (A) Director: Manages school affairs; (B) Director of Academic Affairs: 1. Formulate curriculum; 2. Adjust academic status; 3. Find teachers; 4. Internship guidance; 5. Examine students' grades; (C) Director of Training: 1. Manage students' daily life; 2. Guide students' extracurricular assignments; 3. Cultivate students' spirit and personality; 4. Handle students' attendance and absence; 5. Manage students' rewards and punishments; (D) Director of General Affairs: 1. Manage finances; 2. Handle food and lodging; 3. Draft documents; 4. Keep books; 5. Daily general affairs. (4) Funding: This institute plans to recruit 50 students and provide them with six months of training. The institute will provide food, lodging, books, and clothing, which will cost approximately 1,200 yuan per month, totaling 7,200 yuan in six months. The budget is attached separately. (5) Curriculum: The institute will have eight hours of classes every day. From 8:00 to 9:00 AM is morning exercise, and from 4:00 to 5:00 PM is recreational exercise. The remaining six hours are for learning. The curriculum is prescribed as follows: Party Doctrine (4) (This number is the number of class hours per week, the same below); Boy Scout Training (3); Phonetic Symbols (1); Labor Issues (2); Introduction to Labor Education (2); Trade Union Secretary's Guide (2); Organization and Training of Trade Unions (2); Rudiments of Civil Rights (2); A Brief Account of Revolutionary Memorial Days (1); Research on Imperialism (A Brief History of Anti-Oppression in China) (6); Formalities of Official Documents (Emphasis on Practice) (3); Cooperative Organization (2); Research on the Seven Major Sports (1); Statistical Common Sense (2); Legal Common Sense (2); Political Common Sense (2); Outline of Sociology (2); Outline of Economics (2); Outline of Social Psychology (2). (6) Qualifications of Students: (A) Age: 18 to 35 years old; (B) Character: Upright character and sound physique; (C) Education: 1. Graduates of secondary schools with credentials; 2. Graduates of higher elementary schools who have served for more than three years with solid proof; 3. Those with equivalent education who have served as elementary school teachers for more than two years with solid proof; 4. Those who have served in the Party headquarters for more than one year with solid proof; 5. Those with equivalent education who have worked hard in mass movements with achievements; (D) Party Membership: Formal or probationary member of the Party; (E) Volunteers: 1. Absolutely subject to the Party's command; 2. Must serve the Party for at least two years after graduation; 3. If the job is changed within two years without the special permission of the Party Headquarters, all training costs must be reimbursed; 4. A guarantor must be found at the time of admission to guarantee the above conditions.
