Petition from the Municipal Training Committee Requesting the Central Government to Promptly Order the Resumption of Operations by Nanyang Tobacco Factory 143

The Public Training Committee of the Shanghai Special Municipal Party Department, considering that the abrupt closure of the Nanyang Tobacco Company in this city last year and its failure to resume operations in accordance with the handling methods of Party and government organs, resulting in the sudden unemployment and hardship of thousands of workers at the factory, yesterday specially submitted a petition to the Central Training Department, stating that (the above is omitted) the case was approved by the Secretariat of our Party Department and forwarded to your department's letter No. 8758, hoping that the shutdown dispute of the Nanyang Tobacco Factory would be investigated and a solution would be jointly drafted by the municipal government and submitted to the department for approval. It is hereby ordered to handle it. It has been secretly investigated that the association has previously received a report from Liang Kunli and others, representatives of the unemployed workers of the Nanyang Tobacco Factory, stating that the factory suddenly closed down the Shanghai factory, and all the workers were suddenly unemployed and had difficulty making a living, requesting a quick order to open the factory. It should be a labor-capital dispute, and the Bureau of Social Affairs has been requested to find a way to mediate it quickly. It was then replied that the representatives had come to the meeting one after another to request relief, and then proposed the ninth meeting of the previous association. Since the reorganization of Nanyang Brothers Tobacco Company in the eighth year of the Republic of China, it has earned 3 to 4 million yuan in the five years from the eighth to the twelfth year of the Republic of China, and 2 to 3 million yuan in the four years from the 13th to the 16th year of the Republic of China. Although it lost a total of 4 million yuan in the 17th and 18th years of the Republic of China, it is no less than a drop in the bucket for the company, and there are more than 3,000 employees in the factory. Once unemployed, they will feel difficult to make a living, which will hinder social public security. According to the investigation report, the company did not report to the Party and government organs before closing the Shanghai factory, which is a clear violation of Articles 6 and 7 of the Interim Measures for Retirement Benefits of Employees in this city. The resolutions were: (1) The association believes that the Nanyang Tobacco incident is a problem of suspension of business rather than cessation of business. (2) The Bureau of Social Affairs determines the period of suspension of business based on the actual situation. (3) During the suspension period, the factory should pay workers' living expenses. (4) The money that the factory has paid should be regarded as workers' living expenses and should not be regarded as retirement money. (5) Please order the factory to issue the unpaid maintenance

Page 14

Fee to all workers in accordance with the rules. (6) The above methods should be notified to the workers' delegation. The six handling methods were immediately sent to the Bureau of Social Affairs for quick handling in order to eliminate disputes and prevent future troubles. Later, the Bureau of Social Affairs and the Association repeatedly mediated, but the factory had no sincerity in mediation, so the mediation was terminated. Later, the Bureau of Social Affairs forwarded an order from the Municipal Government to inquire whether the previous resolutions of the Association were based on the workers' requests. The handling methods were based on the workers' requests and the results of the Association's investigation, and should be resolved by the government organs as soon as possible. As for the factory's claim that the case has come to an end and the dispute has subsided, there is no need for the Association to set another handling method, etc., which is not true. Before it is decided whether the business is allowed to cease or suspend, the dispute has not subsided. Moreover, the Interim Measures for Retirement Benefits of Employees in this city have clear regulations on the methods for employers to dismiss employees due to cessation or suspension of business. In order to maintain the authority of the law, the case cannot be said to have subsided because most of the workers have voluntarily received subsidies. It has been repeatedly sent to the Bureau to investigate the previous cause and handle it quickly in order to reach a conclusion as soon as possible. On April 4, Liang Kunli and others, representatives of the factory workers, reported that the factory owner had entrusted other tobacco factories to roll cigarettes as usual, requesting that the factory be ordered to quickly open the factory and resume work in order to maintain their livelihood. A special staff was sent to consult with the Bureau of Social Affairs to determine the methods as follows: (1) Order the factory to submit the factory rules, employment contract, and resumption plan to the Bureau for approval before the end of April. (2) Limit the factory to open the factory and resume work before May 16. (3) If long-term workers who are laid off by the factory after resumption of work have served for two years, they must be paid retirement money of two months per person. (4) If the factory does not resume work by May 16, the factory should pay one-twelfth of the monthly salary as maintenance fee during the extended period. The disputes have been delayed and unresolved after the factory closed down, which is not the right way. The factory owner believes that the business is bleak and it is difficult to fulfill the previously agreed contract. It is true that the workers have been unemployed for three months and their lives are difficult. Therefore, the methods are determined as above and have been ordered by the Bureau to be followed by both parties on record. This is the situation of the association and the Bureau of Social Affairs handling the case. The intention of the association was originally to hope that the factory would follow the rules so that the workers' lives could be maintained, the factory's business could be restored, and the disputes could be resolved from then on. However, the company did not appreciate the hard work of the local authorities in maintaining the industry and protecting the workers, and delayed in complying with it and used excuses to seek to withdraw the order. It is planned to send another letter to the Bureau of Social Affairs to discuss the handling methods. However, after reading the report on the 12th of this month, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce's letter No. 1007 to the Municipal Government contained mostly biased words on the side of the company, and said that third parties could not interfere, etc. It is not known that the local authorities in this city repeatedly ordered the factory to plan to resume work because they did not want the declining industry to be further hit and affect the national economy and people's livelihood. The Ministry of Industry and Commerce does not know the facts of the case and ignores the interim regulations of this city, and makes an affirmative statement based on what the company said. It is considered that it should be corrected. In short, the company's suspension of the Shanghai factory is not reasonable in terms of sentiment and reason. If the resumption of work is feasible, it is only because a few principals are ignorant of the facts and unwilling to open the factory. Therefore, in order to plan the industry of our country and protect the welfare of workers, please ask your department to forward the National Government to order the company to follow the methods determined by the Bureau of Social Affairs of this city to resume work as soon as possible, so as to maintain the political order and eliminate disputes. In order to facilitate the Party, it is hereby presented to the Training Department of the Central Executive Committee.

Collective Discussion of Vegetable Open-Air Weighing Industry 151

Zhou Rongsheng, Qu Jiasheng, Zhu Daozhong, and more than 20 other members of the open-air weighing industry in Shanghai City recently believed that since the opening of trade between China and foreign countries in Shanghai, the concession has gradually expanded and the population has become more and more dense. Therefore, it is almost impossible to find a planting place in the vicinity. It depends on the vendors of vegetables from the nearby villages to meet the market. As a result, the market prices are not consistent and the weights are not the same. Therefore, there are often disputes and disputes that have become a habit. We, the open-air weighing industry, have repeatedly discussed the convenience of landowners and vendors. The only way is to organize a joint office of the same industry so that the buying and selling of vegetables in the market has a certain market price and a certain weight, so that the fraudulent and deceptive people can know themselves and restrain themselves from doing wrong. If there is heavy rain or drought and the source is scarce, the same industry will raise funds to purchase from the producing area at a parity price so that there is no shortage in the market, which is truly a win-win situation. It is heard that it has been decided to set up a joint office of the vegetable industry at No. 29 Ruifu Lane, French Concession, in a suitable location, and to carefully draft the regulations for temporary trial operation. Once it is successfully operated, it will be submitted to the official for filing.

Local News II

River Ching Steamer Escapes from a Hail of Bullets 152

Pirate Ship Failed to Catch Up

One Passenger Injured

The Shanghai Zhengchang Inland River Steamer Bureau, located on the south bank of Bentang Lane Bridge on the North Suzhou River in this city, has a total of three small steamers operating on the Shenhu route: River Ching, River Xing, and Juxing. On the afternoon of the 24th of this month, at 2:00 PM, the River Ching steamer towed four company ships and passenger and cargo ships from the lake to Shanghai. When it reached the Luoxu Tangkou, it was about 9:00 PM on the same evening. Suddenly, it encountered more than 40 pirate ships. The pirates on sentry duty mistakenly thought that the steamer was towing stone ships. When they saw that the towed ships were full of passengers, they realized that it was the Shenhu route steamer. They immediately ordered the steamer to stop, but the River Ching steamer had already sailed dozens of feet away from the pirate ship. The captain of the steamer knew that it was a pirate ship and ignored it. The pirates immediately opened fire with volley guns. The steamer sped forward to escape. The pirate ship followed and opened fire with volley guns. Fortunately, the steamer sped like lightning and the pirates failed to catch up, so they turned back. In this battle, the bandits fired about 50 shots, causing more than 10 gun holes in the last two boards of the Shen Yunquan passenger and cargo ship. A passenger selling mustard greens, Xiao Asan, was shot in the left leg, but the bullet did not penetrate. The steamer sailed to Shanghai yesterday morning. According to the information reported by the company manager, Xiao Asan, who was injured at the time, was taken to Renji Hospital for treatment by car.

Passengers and driver, a total of four people

Twenty packages of smoking paraphernalia in a suitcase

Each offender is separately detained and fined

The blue car is sentenced to be confiscated

On the morning of the day before yesterday, around 10:00 AM, patrol officers from the Dachang Branch of the Baoshan County Public Security Bureau were patrolling on the Shanghai-Taicang long-distance highway when they noticed a blue car carrying four people, including passengers and a driver, speeding north. Finding their behavior suspicious, the officers immediately ordered the car to stop and conducted a search. They discovered twenty packages of opium of varying sizes in a suitcase inside the car. The police then impounded the car, along with the people and the evidence, and took them to the bureau. After questioning by the bureau chief, the suspects identified themselves as: Ma Yiru, 34 years old, from Shandong, residing on a boat in Liuhe, formerly a navigator in the anti-smuggling camp, currently unemployed; Li Jiren, 38 years old, from Shandong, residing in Shanghai's Xiaodongmen, running a cigarette paper shop; Zhang Tielin, 30 years old, from Shanghai, working as an accountant at the Futai Automobile Company on Minquan Road; and Zan Peigen, 31 years old, from Changzhou, working as a driver at the Fuda Automobile Company. The bureau, considering the case related to the transportation and sale of opium, immediately prepared a document and sent it to the County Public Security Bureau for transfer to the Baoshan County Government. Yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM, County Magistrate Wu dispatched Judge Zhang Wei to hold a hearing. Ma Yiru testified that at 8:00 AM the day before yesterday, he and Li Jiren went to the Futai Automobile Company at No. 21 Minquan Road, which was owned by their friend Wu Quangui, and borrowed a car for their own use to drive back to Liuhe. He was carrying a handbag entrusted to him by his friend Lin He, and he did not know that the suitcase contained opium until the police inspection at Dachang revealed the two large and small packages of opium. He did not know the weight. After being taken to the bureau, the Li went with him to Liuhe. The Zhang and Cao were the car company's accountant and driver, respectively, and their remaining statements were evasive. Li Jiren testified that he and Ma were friends. At 9:00 AM this morning, he went to the Futai Automobile Company and called for a car at a price of eleven yuan. He followed Ma to Liuhe to burn incense. A friend named Lin Ming asked them to take a box to Liuhe, and he did not know what was in it. Lin Ming told him to go burn incense. This was his first time, and he had not been there before, and so on. Zhang Shulin testified that he worked as a night accountant at the Futai Automobile Company. He and the driver Cao Peigen went to play. He knew Ma and Li. The car belonged to the owner of the company, Wu Quangui, and was Wu's private car. Cao Peigen testified that they called for a car at 9:00 AM today. He was sleeping upstairs and was not the one who negotiated the price, but rather the accountant Xu. He did not know about the opium, and the box did not smell of opium. He could not ask the guests to open the box for inspection, and so on. After reviewing the statements, Judge Zhang sentenced Ma Yiru to one year and six months in prison with a two-year reprieve and a fine of 1,500 yuan for the crime of intending to sell and transport opium. Li Jiren was sentenced to the same crime with one year and six months in prison with a two-year reprieve and a fine of 1,000 yuan. Zhang Shulin was sentenced to the same crime with one year and six months in prison with a two-year reprieve and a fine of 150 yuan. Cao Peigen was sentenced to the same crime with one year and six months in prison and a fine of 80 yuan. The car was confiscated.

The bridal sedan overturns, the bride is injured

Carriers exhaust themselves propping up the sedan with wood

Rickshaw pullers gather to watch the spectacle

Forgetting themselves, they knock over the sedan

縣民衆敎育館組織剿蠅奪標大會 173

County Public Education Center Organizes Fly-Swatting Competition

Public viewing scheduled for June 15th

In view of the increasingly hot weather and the fact that flies are a medium for spreading infectious diseases, the Shanghai County Public Education Center, recognizing that they must be eliminated as soon as possible to prevent harm, has established regulations and organized a fly-swatting competition. Starting today, notices have been sent to district offices and rural schools, and promotional advertisements have been posted to encourage people in each district to work hard to swat flies. The collection and public viewing will be held on June 15th, and a silver shield will be awarded to the person who swats the most flies. The second and third place winners will also receive considerable prizes. It is hoped that this initiative will eliminate fly infestations to a considerable extent. The guidelines for participating in the competition are as follows: (1) The center will hold a summer hygiene lecture on June 15th and will hold the fly-swatting competition on the same day. (2) Eliminating flies is an important task for summer epidemic prevention. To promote this effort, the center is launching a fly-swatting competition, inviting enthusiastic people from all walks of life to actively catch flies and bring them to the center for public viewing on June 15th. A silver shield will be awarded to the group or individual who catches the most flies, and the second and third place winners will also receive considerable prizes. (3) Public and private groups, agricultural, industrial, and commercial sectors, and private individuals in the six districts of the county are eligible to participate. All captured flies must be sealed in tin cans, wrapped in thick paper, and sealed with adhesive, with the name of the fly catcher or group written on the outside. If not personally delivered, the mailing address must be noted. (4) The results of the fly-swatting competition will be judged by weight, with the highest weight being the first choice. (5) When catching flies, pay attention to the cleanliness of the fly swatter. Use pliers to remove dead flies attached to the swatter and place them in a fixed container. Do not catch flies by hand, and wash your hands each time to avoid infection. The fly swatter should also be rinsed with boiling water from time to time.

Flammable Liquids Must Be Loaded into Insured Cars

Protect Passenger Safety

The Jinghu-Hangyong Railway Police Department has recently issued a notice posted at various stations, stating that flammable liquids are highly flammable and explosive and should be strictly controlled and prohibited. This order, etc., has been issued to the police chiefs of each section to strictly investigate and prohibit, and it is also hereby announced to all passengers that if you are carrying flammable and explosive items, you must report to the station and load them into insured cars in accordance with the regulations, and do not carry them privately in passenger cars to avoid danger and ensure safety. This order is important.

Ms. Dai, a woman from Danyang, lives across from the Dahua Hotel in Zhongde Lane, North Shansi Road. Yesterday afternoon at about 6:30 PM, she was leading her five-year-old daughter Jin Feng and two-year-old son Jin Yi on their way through the mouth of Pentang Lane, Shansi Road. Suddenly, a commercial vehicle with license number 18172 belonging to the Xinglong Automobile Company on Datong Road came and Ms. Dai and her two children could not avoid it and were all injured. Later, the police arrived and sent the mother and three children and the offending driver Chen Genfu to Baolong Hospital and the patrol room respectively. Ms. Dai was injured in the waist and both children were injured in the head, but not seriously.

賣烟者與吸烟者併懲 189

Seller and smoker both punished

A woman named Zhang Wang leased a room upstairs at No. 1019 North Zhejiang Road to sell opium privately. Huisi patrol officer Bai learned of this and went to investigate and arrest her. She and the opium smoker Bao Zhixing were arrested together. Qian Yuechi, who lived downstairs in the house, had a smoking habit and was lying on a couch enjoying the pleasure of smoking, which led to his arrest. The day before yesterday, they were sent to the Special Zone Local Court for questioning by Judge Sun. Zhang Wang, the seller of opium, was sentenced to one month and ten days of imprisonment and a fine of 50 yuan. Bao was sentenced to one month of imprisonment and a fine of 60 yuan. Qian was sentenced to one month of imprisonment and a fine of 100 yuan. The imprisonment portion of the sentences of all three was suspended and the drug paraphernalia was confiscated.

新菜塲之假名歛錢者拘獲四人 190

Four people arrested for collecting money under false pretenses at the new vegetable market

To be sent to court for interrogation this morning

The Municipal Council Police Department recently learned that unscrupulous elements at the new vegetable market at the intersection of Simalu and Zhejiang Road were collecting activity fees of ten yuan per stall from the stallholders. There are 500 stall spaces in the market. If calculated at ten yuan per stall, the amount would be considerable. Recently, some stallholders have paid ten yuan but have not yet obtained a stall space, so they reported it to the Municipal Council Police Department. Yesterday afternoon, the Laozha Patrol Room received a report from an informant that unscrupulous elements who were collecting fees under false pretenses were currently collecting fees at the market. The detectives rushed to the market and arrested four major suspects on the spot. They are scheduled to be sent to the court this morning for trial.

獨子暴死 191

Son dies suddenly

Kicked in the chest

Awaiting doctor's examination

Old mother cries

A widow named Liu Mei, of Wenzhou, who lives above the Baoda firewood and charcoal shop at the corner of Tianji Lane, West Sichuan Road, lost her husband last year. Her only son, Liu Ridong, 13, was an apprentice at the Wanhua Cheng Laundry owned by Zhang Binghao, No. 2, Jiuxing Lane, Juplais Road in the French Concession, who was also from her hometown. He was intelligent and deeply valued by his master. One day two months ago, the apprentice, Liu, was squatting on the floor inside his shop, not knowing what work he was doing, when a guest, Hu Arong (age 28, from Shaoxing), called to Liu and kicked him hard in the chest when he failed to respond. Liu fell back to the ground and spat out blood three times. His master learned of this and sent him to the hospital for treatment, but he returned to work in the shop. Unexpectedly, on the 24th, Liu suddenly died at 2 p.m. The boss reported the death to the French police, who ordered a detective to arrest Hu Arong, the perpetrator. The body was taken to the Tongren Fuyuan Hall for a post-mortem examination. Liu's mother and witness Zhang Binghao were notified. Yesterday, the police reported to the French Court and Judge Zhu oversaw the post-mortem examination. Given the unclear circumstances of the death, he ordered that photographs be taken and that a Western doctor be sent to report the details of the examination to the court before further verification of the body was carried out. After the examination, the body could be buried by the family. Before the examination, the old mother suddenly saw her only son die an unnatural death and wept loudly. Her companions tried to dissuade her and only stopped after the examination was complete. She left despondently.

Mao Leng Store Sues for Overdue Payment 195

Defendant's Store Transfer Content is Complex

Plaintiff Provides 30% Guarantee

The owner of Yi Sheng Chang wool store on Rue de Montauban in the French Concession, represented by a lawyer, filed a lawsuit in the French court, stating that Tong Tai Xing wool store at No. 74 on the same street owed the plaintiff a total of 13,287 taels of silver. Unexpectedly, on the 5th of this month, the store owner's wife, Ms. Ye Sun, privately transferred the store to Heng Ji, operated by lawyers Zhang Ai Kui and Yang Keng, who published a statement in the newspaper and secretly changed the store's name at night, disregarding the debt to the plaintiff. Therefore, the plaintiff urgently filed a lawsuit requesting an emergency measure to temporarily seize the store. They argued that this type of store transfer was completely fraudulent, and in reality, it was still the same business attempting to evade debt, which is legally invalid. They requested a strict investigation of Tong Tai Xing, Heng Ji, and Shao Zhong Ying. Lawyers representing the defendants stated that their clients had a formal contract for the transfer of the store, with lawyers providing proof, with a total price of 11,200 yuan, and four checks from Jun Chang Zhuang could prove the payment. They pointed out that Tong Tai Xing only transferred part of the store to Heng Ji, and Tong Tai Xing still operated part of the business themselves. They questioned why the plaintiff did not investigate clearly before rashly filing a case and requesting a seizure, which was unreasonable, and requested the case be dismissed. Ms. Ye Sun was also represented by a lawyer who argued that the defendant, Ms. Sun, currently resided in the Chinese territory, and the plaintiff's claim was under the wrong jurisdiction, and requested the case be rejected. Judge Gong ordered the plaintiff to provide a 30% guarantee and postponed the case for further review.

Illegal Bamboo Frames and Straw Sheds 196

Demolition Ordered Within a Limited Time

The Shanghai Special Municipality recently received a petition from citizens Wu Hui Tang, Cao Yu Cheng, and others, stating that someone had recently erected bamboo frames and straw sheds at the corner of Heng Tong Road in Zhabei to set up vegetable stalls and collect rent. This type of illegal construction easily leads to fire hazards, and they requested the Public Works Bureau be ordered to demolish them promptly to ensure public safety and prevent fires. After receiving the petition, the Municipal Government ordered the Public Works Bureau to instruct them to demolish the structures within a limited time.

Shanghai-Hangzhou Train Fire Burns Hemp Sacks 197

At 2:10 PM yesterday, more than forty hemp sacks transported from Hangzhou by Yong Xing Transportation Company on behalf of customers the day before were stored on the third platform of the Shanghai South Railway Station on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway. Unexpectedly, locomotive F-17 was dispatched from the locomotive shed and was shunting on the fourth track, preparing to connect with the 24th freight train to Hangzhou, when sparks from the locomotive flew into the hemp sacks. A strong wind caused the fire to blaze up in an instant. Fortunately, the station staff and railway police worked together to extinguish the fire quickly. As a result, twelve hemp sacks were damaged.

Record of Dr. Ma Gu Lie's Lecture 198

Yesterday at 3:00 PM, the Oriental Cultural Society invited its member Dr. Ma Gu Lie to give a public lecture at the French Auditorium, No. 11 Huan Long Road, on "Changes and Characteristics of Asian Culture." In addition to dozens of members of the society, there were about 300 guests, including the wife of President Cai Jie Min of the Academia Sinica. The president of the society, Mr. Li Wei Hou, gave an introductory speech and invited Dr. Ma Gu Lie to take the stage. Dr. Ma Gu Lie lectured entirely in Chinese for two hours, speaking clearly and maintaining his energy throughout. None of the audience members left before the end of the lecture. The lecture was very long and full of essential points, revealing insights that had not been expressed by predecessors. After the lecture, Mr. Li Wei Hou delivered a speech of thanks. A commemorative photo was taken in the garden behind the auditorium. At 5:00 PM, Professor Liu Sui Jiu of Wuhan University and Dr. Ding Zhao Qing invited the Shanghai correspondent of the four major newspapers in Paris, Mr. Laurens, to visit the Chinese Art College exhibition. They all praised the works of the college.

Drunken Man Has His Ear Cut Off 199

Chen Er Da, the son of Ms. Chen Pan, a Changshu woman residing at No. 9 Hua An Fang, North Zhejiang Road, currently works as a partner at the nearby Zhen Hua Hotel. He is 35 years old. The night before last, at around 9:00 PM, he was invited by his uncle-in-law Geng Zhi Qing, his cousin Chen Xing Sheng, and his friend Wang A Gen to a hotel for drinks. Er Da became very drunk. He hired a car to return home first, but somehow, his ear was cut off on the way, and he was covered in blood. His mother saw this and suspected that his uncle-in-law, Geng Zhi Qing, deliberately got her son drunk and lured him into a small alley to cut off his ear. She immediately filed a complaint with the 4th District, 1st Precinct, along with witness Geng Chen (Geng Zhi Qing's wife), accusing Geng and others. After questioning by Director Yao, Geng Chen confessed that Geng Zhi Qing had taken a concubine outside and did not provide for her, so she came to Shanghai to work as a helper. He often came to ask for money, and when she refused, he lured her nephew out, got him drunk, and harmed him. When questioned, Geng and others did not admit to the accusation. All the witnesses were sent to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for further investigation.

Fire on Zhong Xing Road, Zhabei 200

A fire broke out at the Chen He Shun tea leaf box workshop on Zhong Xing Road in Zhabei at around 7:00 PM last night. The fire quickly spread through the roof and to the adjacent Chang Sheng Li and Ren Xie Ji carpentry shop and Qian Feng Ji workshop. Fire brigades from the first, second, and third districts rushed to the scene and worked hard to extinguish the fire, which was brought under control after two hours. It is estimated that three houses and a large amount of wood were destroyed. The arsonist was detained by the patrol police and handed over to the 2nd Sub-precinct of the 5th District Public Security Bureau for investigation.

News from the Art College Exhibition Yesterday 202

The Chinese Art College's teacher and student art exhibition was held yesterday for the second day. As it was Sunday, the number of visitors was very high, exceeding 2,000. Celebrities such as Ye Yu Hu, Wang Yi Ting, and Jing Zi Yuan attended the exhibition and praised the students' pure painting style and their willingness to work hard on the foundations, washing away the rough and unrestrained habits of Shanghai. They greatly admired the teaching methods of the professors. The French Ministry of Education sent Mr. Ma Gu Lie, a special investigator of Chinese higher education, and Mr. Laurens, the Shanghai correspondent of the four major newspapers in Paris and the editor-in-chief of the French Shanghai newspaper, to visit the exhibition with French literary Dr. Ding Zhao Qing. They were received and explained the spirit of Chinese art by professors Liu Sui Jiu, Ma Meng Rong, Zheng Man Qing, Ma Gong Yu, and Fang Jie Kan. Dr. Ma, who has a deep understanding of Chinese literature and art, praised the achievements and promised to give a lecture at the school after his trip to Hangzhou. He also requested to keep the works of Meng Rong, Man Qing, and other teachers and students as souvenirs. It was heard that more than ten pieces of artwork were secured for purchase yesterday. It was also heard that the exhibition period will only last to today and will not be extended.

Salvage Work Being Carried Out at Song Kou 203

Circular from Xi, Inspector of the Customs Marine Department: This inspectorate has found that the Jianghai Customs Tax Department is carrying out salvage work on sunken ships near Wusongkou within the boundary. The details of the situation are listed below. The Kang Tai steamship has sunk in the Changjiang River channel. Its location is 83.5 degrees south-west of the Wusong Lighthouse (according to the compass direction), at a distance of 2.42 English miles. Salvage work began on June 1 of last year and was announced in Circular No. 951. Now work is temporarily suspended and is scheduled to resume on or around June 1 of this year. All ships passing through this area must stay far away from the sunken ship's location and must travel extremely slowly to avoid endangering the divers and hindering the salvage work. To know the location mentioned above, please refer to the Hydrographic Office's Chart No. 1, No. 2, and No. 7 for details. Therefore, all ships should be notified to pay close attention to this announcement and take careful note to avoid negligence. Do not forget, do not neglect. This notice is issued on May 22 of the 19th year of the Republic of China.

Weather Report 210

The Xujiahui Observatory issued a weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stating that the hurricane would move towards the Macclesfield Islands and the Paracel Islands. There is a large cyclone in the northern part of the China Sea. There is a southwest wind north of 35 degrees north latitude, and the wind is calm and directionless to the south. The sky is overcast with occasional rainfall across the country's coasts. The temperature in this city for the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday was a high of 79.0 and a low of 59.0. On the same day last year, the high was 83.5 and the low was 64.6.

Letter to the Editor

To Whom It May Concern:

Thank you for introducing "The Essentials of Humanitarianism" in your newspaper. In recent days, requests for copies have exceeded ten thousand. The initial and second printings of 20,000 copies have been gradually exhausted, but requests continue to pour in. Our factory owner is sparing no expense to continue printing a third edition of ten thousand copies to meet the demand. The printing is currently in full swing, so requests from various places cannot be sent out immediately and must wait for several days. They will be sent out one by one without any omission. However, future requests must include a postal fee of two and a half cents (please note "Request for Book" on the envelope). We hope your newspaper will announce this on our behalf so that those requesting books will not have to wait anxiously. With best wishes for your well-being.

Sincerely,

The General Affairs Department of the Wuxi Shen Xin Third Textile Company

Free Talk

Laugh It Off - A Foreigner 211

Man (staring intently into his lover's eyes): I say, your beautiful eyes are like the shining of the autumn moon, like the twinkling of the spring stars, like the rippling of a clear lake. Besides that, do you have any other good lines to enlighten me?

Woman: Like two diamond heads inlaid on a white gold ring, full of fiery brilliance. This ring is what you have promised me but have yet to bestow upon me.

Female customer: Last time I bought three hams from your store, and they all tasted very good. Do you have the same kind?

Shop assistant: These hanging here are all the finest Jinhua hams, with excellent taste.

Female customer: If these hams were cut from the same pig as the ones I bought last time, then I will buy three more.

A: His cross-eyed look is really unbearable. Once, I suffered a great loss because of it.

B: His cross-eyes are on his own face. What does it have to do with you? How could it cause you to suffer a great loss?

A: That day, someone invited me to a Western-style meal. I happened to be sitting next to him. His cross-eyes were focused on my side, and he ate all the food on my plate.

Chairman Chiang's Leisurely Interest 212

From Jian Nong, sent from Xuzhou:

Chairman Chiang was stationed in Xuzhou at the Longhai North Station. On the morning of the 18th, during a break from military affairs, he went on a casual trip in plain clothes, accompanied by Shao Li Zi, Zhou Fo Hai, and others, leaving the camp train to take a distant view of the suburbs and relax. On that day, after a fresh rain, a slight chill lingered. The Tongshan Normal School Experimental Elementary School was holding its spring sports meet on the playground near the Longhai North Station. The lively young students were eagerly rubbing their fists and preparing to take the field and show off their skills. Chiang stopped to watch and said to the school's teachers and staff: "I will give a considerable prize to the first place in each group to encourage the children." It turned out that the morning's sports program was track and field, and the students had been divided into four groups, A, B, C, and D, who would compete in turn. Some of the students recognized Chiang and told each other, and the whole venue cheered to welcome Chairman Chiang. Chiang nodded in response. After the final races, Chiang distributed awards, including a certificate for Guo Dian Cheng, first place in Group A, with the words "Victory" written on it; a certificate for Li Yun Cheng, first place in Group B, with the words "Progress" written on it; a certificate for Ding Zhen Dong, first place in Group C, with the words "Success" written on it; and a certificate for Liu Cheng Xin, first place in Group D, with the words "Swiftness" written on it. The certificates were all made of brocade and the words were written by Chairman Chiang himself. He then ordered his attendants to return to the camp train and bring a large number of biscuit cans and canned goods to donate to the children of the whole school. He also gave a speech, saying: "The physique of the Chinese people has never been strong and is often ridiculed by foreigners. I hope that you young students will exercise every day to make your bodies strong, so that not only will you not be looked down upon by foreigners, but our strength against foreign powers will also be increased invisibly. What worries should the country have? What worries should there be about not being able to defeat imperialism? The National Games will be held in Beijing next April. You young students should practice hard and go there to participate. I will be waiting for you in Beijing. We are currently in the period of suppressing the rebellion, and military affairs are very busy. As soon as the military affairs on the front lines are over, I will go to your school again for a deep talk." His attitude was gentle and his smile was kind. He also strolled along the grass path, admiring the willow branches and mountain scenery for an hour before returning to the camp.

The Stone-Throwing Festival - Gu Shi De 213

In our county, every year during the abolished lunar calendar Arbor Day, there is a custom of throwing stones with the neighboring village of Liu She. According to the elders, this tradition has been passed down for more than sixty years. It must be held once a year, otherwise, it will not be auspicious. Liu She is close to Taihu Lake, while our county is slightly southwest, but they are very close to each other. The peach and willow trees at the end of the villages are connected, and the bank of Taihu Lake is used as the war zone. On that day, tourists are like clouds, and red-clad men and green-clad women are like butterflies flitting back and forth. The barren hills are full of spectators. At noon, the banks begin to be bombarded with stones. At first, stone fragments are thrown remotely to correspond to the traditional custom of warding off disasters. By the time of the late afternoon, there are many spectators on both sides, and the number of stone-throwers who automatically join in increases greatly. Each person throws sharp stones bravely at each other. Those who are unfortunately hit by stones are wounded and bleed. The winners are elated, and the spectators of both villages shout according to the victory or defeat of their own side. The foolish state is very interesting. They must fight fiercely until dusk before each side returns home. The annual stone-throwing festival is thus announced to be over.

Those who heard of it praised Chairman Chiang's composure.

(A Retort)

Snippets from the Four Universities English Speech Contest - Hua Hua 214

Jiaotong, Fudan, Jinan, and Guanghua Universities held the English speech contest on the 21st at Fudan University. As a result, Jiaotong University won the team first place, and Ms. Wang Heng Ling, a female student from Jiaotong University, won the individual first place. Now, I will extract and record the snippets from the competition.

Dr. Hu's witty remarks provoked laughter: On that day, Dr. Hu Shi served as the chairman. Each actor who stepped onto the stage had to say "Chairman" and bow to him. Dr. Hu responded with a smile. After the performance, the chairman usually had a few closing remarks. Dr. Hu took the opportunity to make witty remarks, saying that today, he had nothing to do but take up the seat of the chairman, which could only be described as "Chairman" in English and not in Chinese, because he was only sitting on a chair and doing nothing, just as the English "Chairman" can be translated literally as "chair-sitting person." The audience burst into laughter.

The joy and suffering of the judges varied: The judges on that day were Chen Ting Rui, Ou Yuan Huai, and Bauer (editor-in-chief of the "Millard's Review"). To prevent the judges from consulting with each other, the judges' seats were spaced far apart. However, the venue was quite large, and the judges sitting in the back had to concentrate their thoughts and listen carefully to be able to hear clearly. One of the judges told others afterward that he had used up a lot of his ear power today, and he was quite indignant about the joy and suffering varying among the other judges.

Sharing honors equally: This competition only took four places. As a result, Wang Heng Ling (Jiaotong) was first, Liu Sheng Qi (Guanghua) was second, Zhu Zi Fen (Fudan) was third, and Lin Qing Chi (Jinan) was fourth. Each of the four universities that participated won a place, and no one was left out. Some said that this could be described as sharing honors equally. The beauty scheme can only be used once: In last year's Mandarin competition, a female student from Jinan won first place. This year, that student did not win an award. The audience all said that the beauty scheme had failed. This time, Jiaotong again added a female student and won the award. Therefore, when some bored members of the audience were leaving, they shouted loudly (warning Jiaotong that the beauty scheme can only be used once, take the previous incident in Jinan as a warning), and so on. In fact, Ms. Wang's participation in the speech was not from this session, but had been for the first and second time. Only this session did she win the award.

What he has learned not only obtains the appearance but also the spirit, and his exquisite works even surpass the ancients. He is truly worthy of praise for surpassing his predecessors. For example, the peonies, peonies, lotuses, chrysanthemums, pomegranates, and crabapples he made this time are simple, elegant, and full of unconstrained interest, which is already enough to make people marvel. His imitation of Zhao Zi Gu's daffodils is graceful and even more lovely. The figures, such as Mei Du, Lao Zi, Lu Shang, Guan Ling Yin Xi, Ji Kang, Dong Po, and Zhong Kui, are dignified and leisurely, allowing viewers to leisurely recall the past and feel awe and respect. They are not only remarkable in terms of brush and ink. He has the most landscapes, and they are also the most exquisite. Miscellaneous Records of Mei Lanfang's Tour in America 216

On April 17th, departed from Chicago by train, traveling to the highest point of the Rocky Mountains. The weather was extremely warm, and the flowers and trees were in full bloom, creating a beautiful and unparalleled landscape.

On the 24th, arrived in San Francisco at 5 PM. Upon disembarking, several thousand people were at the station to greet him. The number of people watching the spectacle was about thirty to forty thousand, a truly unprecedented scene. The Mayor of San Francisco, the President of the Chamber of Commerce, the Chinese Consul-General in San Francisco, and the President of the Chinese Chamber of Commerce all personally came to the station to welcome him. A great many people presented flowers. The Mayor gave a speech on the spot, delivering a welcoming address. After the speech, Wanhua and the Mayor rode together in a large open-top car, led by the city's band. The car we were in, as well as the cars of those welcoming us, followed in a continuous line for about a mile. Each car was fully adorned with the flags of both China and America. A banner of welcome was prominently displayed in front of Wanhua's car. It happened to be Sunday, and many of the stores in the southern district were closed, so the spectators filled the roads, causing traffic to be blocked, and all removed their hats as a sign of respect. The band played music as we slowly proceeded through the bustling streets to Chinatown, causing traffic to be completely stopped. More than a dozen police officers on motorcycles directed everything back and forth. After arriving at the welcome venue, it was already a sea of people. The Mayor's speech briefly stated: "I originally had other important matters today, but I deliberately put them aside and rushed to the station to welcome him, because Mr. Mei's visit to America has indeed greatly increased the friendship between China and America. Moreover, the Chinese community in San Francisco accounts for half of the city's construction efforts. Mr. Mei's art is profound. I welcome him from head to toe with sincere enthusiasm and dare to represent the entire city, the entire state, and the entire nation in welcoming him," and so on. Wanhua's reply contained the most persuasive words, saying, "The feeling I have upon arriving in San Francisco this time is that everyone always thinks of the Pacific Ocean as separating China and America. However, I believe that the Pacific Ocean was naturally created to connect China and America." At this point, there was thunderous applause from the audience.

On the 21st, Wanhua visited the Mayor at the City Hall. When the Municipal Council learned of the visit, they immediately suspended the Municipal Council meeting and changed it into a welcoming reception, inviting Wanhua to sit in the chairman's seat. A council member gave a long welcoming speech. After the speech, Wanhua gave a reply speech lasting several tens of minutes. The speech was translated, recorded by a stenographer, and preserved forever. Before departing, he took a group photo with the council members as a memento.

On the 23rd, the women's association with voting rights held a tea party. Upon his arrival, everyone stood up and welcomed him with utmost sincerity. More than two hundred people attended the meeting that day.

On the 24th, it was the state-wide women's association tea party, with three hundred people in attendance. Only one seat was provided for Wanhua, while everyone else stood. There were also speeches given.

It is now planned to perform for seven days at the foreign theater here and five days at the Chinese theater. After the performances, they will go to Los Angeles to perform for ten days and study movies in Hollywood along the way.

Da Dizi Fusheng must also completely prostrate himself. What's even more wonderful is that he did fifteen sketches of the Diamond Mountains. Daqian enjoys travel. Having already left Mount Emei, descended the Wu Gorge, stayed at Lingyin Temple, ascended Mount Tai, traveled north to the borderlands, and toured Wu and Yue in the south, last year he also traveled throughout Shilla and Baekje, exhausting the beauty of the Diamond Mountains. Therefore, his brushwork has become more divine. The Diamond Mountains are so prominent, strange, and steep, beyond the imagination. The help of the landscape is why painters must travel thousands of miles. Daqian had never painted Shi Xi before, but after casually creating two paintings, he rendered the bald remnants colorless. We mediocre people can only burn the inkstones in the burial mound to avoid being ashamed to die. Daqian's nature is scattered. Sometimes he doesn't write a single stroke for dozens of days, but when the mood strikes, he paints freely and vividly, like a fierce wind and torrential rain, making a rattling sound. He can produce dozens of paintings in a day. Truly, he is unfathomable. He can be called a prodigy of the painting world.

A Record of Visiting the Chinese Literary and Artistic School by Qingping 217

I have been a guest in Peiping for a long time. Yesterday, I returned to Shanghai to visit my old friend Manqing at Weixue Cottage. It has been five years since our last meeting. After exchanging greetings and reminiscing about the past, we each shared our feelings about life. Manqing led me to visit the Chinese Literary and Artistic School. The school building is secluded and elegant, with bright windows and clean tables, long grass and fragrant flowers, which is quite in line with the artistic concept. Ancient and modern paintings are hung in the room, all of which are the calligraphy and paintings of famous artists. In the Chenxi Pavilion, ancient books fill the shelves, all of which are exquisitely engraved editions. The "Cefu Yuangui", "Yuhai", "Taiping Yulan", and other books each have more than a thousand volumes, which is especially rare in other schools. Manqing then took out the works of his disciples and invited me to evaluate them. I believe that the students at this school have made such rapid progress in just one semester, thanks to the teaching of their teacher. Now, after briefly observing the achievements of each student, I know that the relationship between teacher and student is deep. Our country's literature and art originated thousands of years ago. Since the import of European culture, the national arts have been relegated to the status of vassals. Recently, society has begun to pay more attention to the national arts, but they are still as rare as phoenix feathers and unicorn horns. My friend Manqing braved the thorns and established an art school. His painstaking efforts are truly commendable and valuable. Moreover, he has also received the assistance of Ye Yufu, Yu Youren, Chu Minyi, and other gentlemen to maintain and support the school, so that the foundation of the school can be consolidated. Is this not the good fortune of the students of this school? It is heard that a teacher-student exhibition will be held at the Ningbo Fellow Association on that day. It is estimated that there will be four or five hundred works. The spring breeze and peach and plum blossoms will gather in one hall, with colorful lights and a dazzling scene, which will surely delight and dazzle the viewers. To promote our country's inherent culture lies in this, lies in this!

Warmth in the Heart (200 Bao Tianxiao) 218

Chapter Eleven: Emerald Locks and Pearly Hairpins, a Beautiful Woman Returns; a Talented Man's Azure Tent and Crimson Curtains, a Famous Courtesan Marries into a Prominent Family

Zuo Shichen asked, "So, have you already bought them?" Liu Xingxu said, "Almost. I said I would buy them, and I paid him two hundred yuan as a deposit, because I haven't received the translation fee of one thousand yuan yet. After I receive it, I can hand over the money, and then I can take the things." Zuo Shichen said, "This is a happy thing. Do you want to send these two things to the woman's house first, to your fiancée?" Liu Xingxu said, "Our Suzhou custom is to send a large platter once a month before the wedding, and all six rituals are sent on that day. I also want to attach these two things to the day I send the large platter." Zuo Shichen said, "So, everything is according to Suzhou wedding customs?" Liu Xingxu said, "Not necessarily. We are following our Suzhou customs. If they are not satisfied and want to follow Huzhou customs, we will listen to them. Fortunately, I am completely in charge of this wedding. My father is not in charge of my affairs, so I will do my best." Time passed like flowing water. In the blink of an eye, it was time for Liu Xingxu's wedding. As a result of Xingxu's efforts in recent years, he handled it very perfectly. He originally had a wide range of acquaintances. Just counting his classmates, there were dozens in Shanghai. In addition, there were quite a few scattered in various places. All Chinese celebrations and condolences are often regarded as major events. Among relatives and friends, even people who don't usually interact will always come to the celebrations and condolences. There is also a reason: it depends on your own social life. If you yourself don't socialize much, people will be lazy. If you are a person who enjoys socializing, people can't help but come. This is called reciprocity. Liu Xingxu is a person who likes to socialize. He goes to every celebration and condolence, no matter how busy he is. Therefore, now that he has encountered his own happy event, people also need to come and respond. On that day, he borrowed the large hotel of Yipinxian and invited Tang Zhaoyi as the wedding officiant. The guests filled the door and it was very lively. When it came to the wedding, everyone crowded to see the newlyweds. That Miss Fang was truly graceful and elegant, and she and Liu Xingxu could be called a perfect match, a talented man and a beautiful woman, a good match made in heaven. It's a pity that Liu Xingxu has been tired recently. The root of his illness has not been removed. During this honeymoon, he took a month's leave from the bookstore because they didn't go on a honeymoon trip. Therefore, he still went to the newspaper office in the evening once in a while. He still had to come out once a day and couldn't hide at home all day long. However, he came home much earlier than usual. There was also one more thing. Before he got married, he also liked to eat and drink and call for courtesans. Since he got married, he has also stopped doing this. His friends asked him if he wasn't keeping his new wife's rules after marrying her?

Major Turmoil in the Gold Market Last Week 220

Silver tax issues cause disturbances.

Speculative trading is aimless.

High and low: 15 taels and 5 qian.

Result: Increase of 2 taels.

The gold market was unusually chaotic last week, with significant fluctuations, often rising or falling by five or six taels. The proposal by the national government to collect import taxes on silver in cash caused rumors and disputes, creating panic among the industry. The atmosphere in the market was confused, and speculative trading was aimless. Overall, the market was disturbed by the air, creating turmoil. On Monday, it reached an unprecedented peak of 528 taels and 5 qian. On Wednesday, it plummeted, nearly collapsing to 513 taels (although the black market only reached 502 taels). The market stabilized by the weekend. Although the British and American silver markets and exchange rates had set new records, they were not correlated with the gold price and were almost inversely proportional. However, the result was slightly higher than the previous Saturday. The details of the past six days are summarized below:

Early in the week (19th), large bars of silver trended lower, and the exchange market contracted by half a notch. The internal market was strong, but the gold price was extremely chaotic. The market fluctuated by more than 9 taels. Buyers were excited, and the early market jumped to a new peak of 528 taels and 5 qian. However, after rumors spread that passports were required for cash imports, it fell sharply. The market closed more than 20 taels lower. The next day, the market was even more chaotic. Due to the rumor that the silver tax would be implemented on a trial basis for six months, panic arose. The market opened with a drop of six or seven taels, and then suddenly fell to 513 taels (although the black market outside the arena only reached 12 taels). At noon, it was learned that a Reuters report stated that the tax could be avoided, and it immediately rebounded, soaring by ten taels. The market closed soft, as large holders sold. The difference between the high and low was eleven taels and a half that day. On Wednesday, the low price of large bars of silver did not move. The rumor that the silver tax was about to be implemented again opened at a lower price. After hearing that the black market had reached 502 taels, the market jumped five or six taels due to buyer activity. The market closed at around 18 taels. The next day, although the large bars and exchange rates contracted, the internal prices were initially strong and then softened. Therefore, the gold market went from firm to weak. In the early morning, it was 24 taels and 5 qian, but then it plummeted by eight or nine taels. Throughout the day, there was a fluctuation of 9 taels. On Friday, the market was calm, but there was still a fluctuation of 5 taels and a half. The government denied the tax, and the people's hearts were firm. On Saturday, the market fluctuated by 4 taels and 2 qian in half a day. However, the large bars returned to their length, and the exchange rate was clearly loose but secretly tight. Therefore, the gold price was 519 taels, which was 2 taels higher than the previous Saturday. The high and low prices for this week were 15 taels and 5 qian. Silk Sales Are Booming This Week 225

More than 30,000 packages of spot goods opened.

It is said that the buyers are powerful because the factory is tightening up and will not let go of the opportunity. Therefore, they have the ability to hold on for a long time. Scattered households saw that the environment had improved and had to get on with it. The buyers were assisted by this and their attitude became stronger. On the one hand, they increased their purchases this month. Therefore, the closing price of the standard yarn on Saturday was still very high. However, the current inventory has not been sold out, and there is no power to rise sharply for the time being. If the purchases from all parties continue to come, the future will continue to rise. In short, after this batch of business started to improve, the burden on each factory was reduced. For a while, it was not easy to tend towards a small surface. US Sales Launched, Silk Prices Turned to Rise 228

The silk market in Shanghai turned from tired to rise in the middle of last week. The reason was that the foreign exchange rate changed drastically at the beginning of the week, and the foreign silk sales did not move. European dealers watched and waited, and there was no possibility of progress in the market. By the second half of the week, the exchange rate had turned firm and US sales were launched. The price of silk in New York was reported to be rising, and the silk electricity gradually turned to Shanghai. US, French, and other dealers successively sold and purchased Shanghai white factory goods. Each manufacturer said that the new cocoon harvest in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces this year was poor and the price of cocoons was not cheap. The silk cost was still expensive, and they had to sell the time silk. They insisted that they would not sell at a loss. As a result, 300 packs of new and old Tongjie Shanghai factory goods were traded in June, and the price of silk rose sharply by 230 taels. The price of overseas Chinese silk rose by a different amount. 700 packs of old silk were shipped out last week. Continuing Decline in White Rice Prices 229

Yesterday, deliveries to Zhabei from the river amounted to only about ten shipments, and sales in various stores were sluggish. Sales of northern rice were especially slow, because the end of the month and the Dragon Boat Festival were approaching, and stores were inevitably taking a wait-and-see approach due to various procedural issues. Therefore, only a small amount of retail sales and some local street trading took place. High-quality rice was still priced steadily, but special grades were only between $20.05 and $20.06. Medium-grade and sub-grade fresh northern rice varied in price and quality, with some being processed and others remaining in their original state, with a price fluctuation of about half a cent. Medium-grade and sub-grade aged rice was not only priced lower but also no one was buying it. However, the river had the largest stock of this type of rice, so trading was sparse throughout the day. High-quality Bo Rice remained stable, while other grades showed signs of fatigue. Although deliveries were scarce, sales were not high. Because medium-grade and sub-grade rice were mostly removed, high prices remained at $20. The Yangdu short-grain rice market continued to be quiet, with sales mainly consisting of foreign rice. Market trading was unusually quiet and fluid. As the Dragon Boat Festival approached, deliveries slightly increased, but buyers were unusually cautious. Although trading volume was not weak, prices often varied according to batches. Therefore, ordinary rice remained around $18.50.

Sources to the Shanghai South districts were scarce, with only a few shipments, and the trend remained normal. Both Xibei northern rice and Su Tongji rice were in short supply, and sales were brisk. All day, only local street sales made slight progress, and there was no significant decline in large orders. High-quality Chang rice was $20, and Su rice was $19. Thin early rice from Songjiang, Sijing, Xitang, Qingjiao, and other areas in the South continued to decline, and sales showed no development. Only high-quality early rice was slightly active, so prices were somewhat adjusted. The market situation was very weak, and Yangdu short-grain rice showed a slight decline, with sales slightly improving and prices remaining stable. The flow of both Tumen rice and Yin rice was rare, and the situation was mediocre. High-quality Yin rice was priced at $17.12.

Slight Turnaround in the Tung Oil Market 230

After the price of white tung oil from foreign firms in Hankou fell to 22.8 taels, Sichuan tung oil opened at 21.3 taels, and Tung tung oil opened at 20.06 taels, all from customer orders. However, repeated price drops caused significant losses for customers, so customers with strong capital generally adopted a strategy of waiting and seeing. Various foreign firms, seeing that further price drops were unlikely in the short term, completed transactions for more than 1,000 tons over the past week, with prices remaining at 22.8 and 22.85 taels. Merchants' inventories were not high, and the sudden fire at Demao Warehouse resulted in losses of over 10,000 dan. Spot oil in the market was in short supply. According to yesterday's Hankou telegram, Wuxiang tung oil had increased to 20.08 taels, and the market seemed to be slightly turning around, with a bit more activity than before. However, foreign firms remained between 22.8 and 22.9 taels, lacking sufficient momentum and not allowing for a rapid rise. There would only be a large drop followed by a small rebound.

Unabated Rise in Eastern Galvanized Iron Prices 231

Recent trading in eastern galvanized iron has been very active, with strong demand from various ports along the Yangtze River and provinces like Fujian and Zhejiang. Local street trade has also been widespread, so daily transactions total 6,000 to 7,000 sheets. However, after the continuous rise of the Eastern Exchange Rate, there have been very few new orders. Because supplies are scarce, the market is very strong, and prices are continuously rising. Currently, 3'x7' sheets are estimated at 98 cents per sheet, and 3'x6' sheets are 77.5 cents, an increase of 0.5 cents compared to before. As the Eastern Exchange Rate is unlikely to ease, and there may be few future deliveries, it is unlikely that prices will soften.

Youth Corner

Mr. Ying Yunwei, the Director I Know by Wu Zhen 232

Since our (Lady Windermere's Fan) was performed at school and in Shanghai, I have deeply come to know this good teacher, Mr. Ying Yunwei. If our performance was a success, then we can only say that it was entirely Mr. Ying's success, because this was entirely the result of Mr. Ying's hard work and guidance in February.

I don't know what kind of power he has that made more than a dozen of us actors obey and admire him. Although he is just a very young youth, we became friends with him as soon as we met him on the first day. Although he is our most powerful director, he is very kind to us. Even if he is angry sometimes, we can see his fiery heart in his angry face. He treats our affairs as his own, sacrificing the company's holidays, and sacrificing a whole year's holiday and Christmas holiday. He worked hard at school to direct our work. As a result, he caught a bad cold from running around in the ice and snow for days and fell ill. When we went to see him, he was still saying (You have to read the script very well. As soon as I get better, I will rehearse for you and take care of all the backstage and front-of-house arrangements for the performance). He is so enthusiastic and sincere to us that we are almost moved to tears. Fortunately, he recovered in a few days. After recovering, he did not recuperate but worked even harder, so that we got a lot of fun from the school performance, and we also got a considerable estimate from the performance in the Central Auditorium. He did not know how much energy and time he lost for our performance this time, but he did not regret it. Moreover, after each performance, he was as happy and cheering as we were. Ah, he is truly a lover of art and a supporter of drama.

Recently, he has been working even harder to promote the performance of Shakespeare's plays in Chinese Mandarin. He has selected Shakespeare's masterpiece, The Merchant of Venice, and asked Mr. Gu Zhongyi to translate it. I don't want to say anything about this script and translation, I just want to talk about Ying Xian's efforts in directing this play. He has studied the costumes in the play - the costumes of the 16th century - and the customs of Venice at that time, even down to a pair of gloves and a candlestick. He does not want to be like the current Chinese stage plays, which rely only on fantasy and speculation to estimate the costumes and customs of people hundreds of years ago. He wants to do his volunteer work seriously and introduce Shakespeare's plays to us.

Fudan Student Army Grand Review (Photo by Xiao Junhou)

At the same time, he also wants to accurately introduce the customs and culture of Europe in the 16th century to us. This is truly something worthy of our attention, admiration, gratitude and praise. As for his directing methods, the strict selection of actors, and the precision of the scenery, it goes without saying. I boldly and arbitrarily say (This time he is bound to have a great success (May 1, at Shanghai University)

The Story of World Literature (161 by John Macy, translated by Hu Zhongchi)

Chapter 41 German Literature After Goethe 237

Now, let us look at the works of German poets and prose writers who have been recognized as having ability, with what deep consideration and what enthusiasm they are laboriously following the shining certainty - Goethe

Many literary, intellectual, and political motives in German literature urged the rise of the Romantic school and determined its nature. Germany, fragmented and powerless, lay at the feet of France. It was only natural that poets and idealists tended in their dreams to the medieval empire bearing the name of Germany. And this led them to Gothic and Catholic churches, to the architectural departments of Nuremberg, the cathedrals of Cologne and Strasbourg, to the love poets of the Old High German era, the monster-infested forests, and the folk songs and legends of rivers and valleys. Mixed with this motive was a philosophical motive. Thinkers born after Kant gradually purified the difficult world of reality, until Fichte declared that it was only a projection of the creative spirit of mankind. In this way, poets have the right to dream, only dream, depict that dream, and that is enough.

The Romantic school did not produce any solid artistic works. Thanks to Schlegel, Tieck, and others' translations of Shakespeare, and thanks to the linguistic labor of the Grimm brothers, it permanently enriched the world of knowledge. The articles are all fragments, mainly because the influence on European literature directly or indirectly is important. Only in terms of lyrical poetry did the Romanticists do first-class work. Novalis' (Fragments) become profound books, but these are only fragments. Hoffmann's stories are not listed as first-class literature. Novalis, Brentano, Eichendorff, Hölderlin, Uhland, and Rückert's lyrical poems are beautiful, and these poems, like Heine's lyrical poems, were composed by Schubert, Schumann, Franz, Brahms, etc. and were then known to the world.

Romantic lyric poetry has a long life, which is maintained in the sad tones of Nikolaus Lenau, and later in the lyric works of Eichendorff, which were made more famous by the composition of Hugo Wolf. This reached its highest point in the two or three flawless poems of Theodor Storm.

Three important figures emerged more or less directly from the Romantic school: Schopenhauer and two playwrights, both Prussians and Austrians, Heinrich von Kleist and Franz Grillparzer. Schopenhauer is famous as the classical interpreter of pessimism. He believes that the sum of the pain of life completely exceeds everything that is expected, equates the biological and spiritual will to live with evil, and declares asceticism and infatuation with art as the only ways of wisdom. The reason for adding him to this literary story is because not only his main work (The World as Will and Representation), but also all his small works, especially the two volumes of essays, are beautiful prose. He provided rich hints for literary linguistics and art music.

In his youth, the self-taught Kleist left behind a few plays and short stories, which gradually increased in value. He is modern. He abandoned the hackneyed tragic psychology and led us into the obscure inner struggles that take place in people's hearts. His (Prince of Homburg) is a beautiful comedy (The Broken Jug), and a few stories like (Michael Kohlhaas) belong to the earliest records in any literature. That is, the Austrian playwright Franz Grillparzer, the most famous, who, although often sickly, convincingly and exhaustively describes an unusually high degree of psychological situation, is far more of a poet and far less of a psychologist than Kleist. More precisely, he is also a Romanticist. His psychology is often close to modern people, but his plays, no matter where he chooses the background of the action, are always essentially human fairylands of plays. His political theory, like his motives, is poetry. Romantic asceticism struggles with high emotion in him, and the traces of that struggle appear in the treatment of all the allegories he constructs. He is not modern. He has no intelligence, but these beautiful, legendary, and brilliant plays - (Sappho) (Golden Fleece) (Dream is Also Life) (Libussa) (Love and the Waves of the Sea) - are bewitching things.

It has been pointed out that Romanticists are dreamers, conservatives, and often Catholics. Not long after the July Revolution broke out, freedom, which had been temporarily hidden since the Battle of Waterloo, redeveloped. A group of writers known as (Young Germany) appeared, who had a more realistic temperament and more liberal ideas. Few of them left immortal works. It is enough to mention the name of Ludwig Börne, the author of a magnificent pamphlet. We can immediately go on to talk about the Romanticists, and the sons of the revolution, the dreamers, and the realists, filled with hopes and enthusiasm for the freedom of mankind, singing the glory of the fairyland, and the misfortunes of the Silesian weavers who, like Hauptmann, made him immortal, the Jew and the German Heine. To talk about Heine, a figure who, until today, has been at the center of the storm of controversy in Germany, like a pendulum, with European influence, significance and fame.
